League of Nations Advisory Committee 15

Yesterday's Meeting Accepted the United States' Reply

To Discuss the Rehe War and Arms Embargo

The League of Nations is Quite Satisfied with the US Reply

(Geneva) The Advisory Committee established by the League of Nations General Assembly to handle the Sino-Japanese dispute convened here this afternoon. The meeting was purely a formality, its sole purpose being to accept the United States' reply regarding its participation in the committee's work. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

(Geneva) The recently organized Far East Affairs Advisory Committee of the League of Nations will convene tomorrow to discuss the progress of the Rehe situation. (Guomin Dian [National Telegram] on the 14th)

(Geneva) Here in Geneva, the US reply is viewed with considerable satisfaction. Official circles believe the United States will participate more fully and effectively than during previous collaborative efforts. Granting Minister Wilson the authority to express opinions at any time and consult with committee members is seen as the maximum extent of participation the US government can permit. Most League of Nations personnel recognize that the United States' statement of reserving independent judgment is merely an idealistic position. Since all international agreements require Senate approval, no resolution can bind the United States. The Advisory Committee will reportedly discuss only the replies from the Soviet Union and the United States, as well as the proposed arms embargo, at its meeting tomorrow. (Guomin Dian [National Telegram] on the 14th)

(Washington) The US government has notified the British government that the US President is making every effort to ensure Congress promptly takes the necessary measures to allow the President to prohibit the export of arms to any country. Under Secretary of State Phillips told British Ambassador Lindsay that President Roosevelt would soon strongly urge Congress to grant him the power to prohibit arms exports for application during international conflicts. Roosevelt's request to Congress strengthens the State Department's reply to the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

(London) According to news from Washington, after the US government decided to cooperate with the League of Nations Advisory Committee in handling issues concerning the Far East, it seems likely to take a further step soon, granting diplomatic recognition to the Soviet government. This news has caused great concern here. Another Washington news report states that it is worth noting that the United States is considering not only the economic benefits that could be gained from the re-establishment of US-Soviet relations. The Manchester Guardian welcomes the United States' decision to join the Advisory Committee and states that if the Roosevelt government endeavors to achieve a unified refusal to supply arms to acknowledged aggressor nations, it will also be sufficient to uphold justice. (Reuters dispatch on the 15th)

Japan's Notification of Withdrawal from the League of Nations 16

Said to be Issued on the 24th

(Tokyo) Japan's notification of withdrawal from the League of Nations will be issued on the 24th of this month. When the Japanese government decides to submit the notification of withdrawal, it will simultaneously publish a statement regarding the Japanese government's position. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has already completed drafting the statement, the main points of which are as follows: 1. Although the Imperial Government is forced to withdraw from the League of Nations, its spirit of respecting peace remains unchanged, and it will continue to cooperate with other nations to jointly promote world peace. 2. The government will appropriately cooperate with the League of Nations' disarmament conferences and other cultural, economic, and peaceful endeavors in the capacity of a non-member state. 3. Regarding "Manchukuo," the government will consistently act according to its belief that it is an independent state, assist its development, and hope that other nations will also treat it with goodwill and assistance, promptly recognizing its independence. 4. The government earnestly desires to quickly restore friendly relations with China and provide friendly assistance in its domestic reorganization. At the same time, it hopes that China will recognize "Manchukuo" and adopt a policy of reorganizing Sino-Japanese-Manchukuo relations. (Dentsu dispatch on the 15th)

Matsuoka in London Propagates Establishing a Tripartite Treaty among Britain, America, and Japan 17

To Replace the Former Anglo-Japanese Alliance

London—Matsuoka, Japan's chief representative to the League of Nations, stated to the press today that American, British, and Japanese politicians should consider negotiating a tripartite treaty to replace the old Anglo-Japanese Alliance. (Guomin Dian [National Telegram] on the 15th)

Tokyo—The Japanese government distributed to the Privy Council's review committee an attached document to the inquiry regarding the League of Nations notification, namely the handling of various matters after the withdrawal notification (excluding mandated territories). The main points are as follows: 1. For the two years after the notification of withdrawal, although having the rights and obligations of a League member, representatives will be absent from the General Assembly and Council, according to custom. 2. There is an obligation to pay the League of Nations' expenses for the two years from the notification of withdrawal until the expiration date. 3. League of Nations staff are appointed by the Secretary-General with the consent of the Council, so the League of Nations has only an employment relationship with that individual, without any direct relationship with their home government. There is no difference because their home country is a League member or non-League member, so Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations has no impact on the status of its staff. Therefore, the Japanese government will not interfere in the promotion or demotion of Japanese staff, allowing them freedom, but if there are voluntary resignations, measures will be taken to provide relief. Also, methods of cooperation with various specialized agencies of the League of Nations after the Japanese government's notification of withdrawal: (1) Consider carefully the internal and external subtleties of the situation at the time of withdrawal. While advancing the "Manchurian" policy, adopt a fair attitude towards European, American, and Russian relations, avoiding the occurrence of incidents, while participating sincerely in general peace affairs to alleviate internal and external anxieties. (2) Although not attending the political General Assembly and Council, still participate and cooperate in other peaceful endeavors, unless there is a special change in the situation. (3) In addition, still participate in the Mandates Committee, the International Office of Public Health, the International Air Navigation Committee, the International Hydrographic Bureau, the Straits Committee, the Communications Conference, and the Central Opium Committee. (4) Still participate in the International Economic and Financial Conference. (5) Still participate in the International Labour Conference. (Dentsu dispatch on the 15th)

(Tokyo) At 11:20 AM today, the Privy Council convened in the East Pavilion of the Imperial Palace to discuss the results of the review of the consultation on withdrawing from the League of Nations. It was decided that the first review committee would be held at the Privy Council Office at 1:30 PM on the afternoon of the 16th. It is feared that the submission of the case to the plenary session will be on the 22nd, which is the regular meeting day. (Dentsu dispatch on the 15th)

(Tokyo) The draft resolution on Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations is under review in the Privy Council. The full text is approximately two thousand characters, making the review difficult. Today, the Second Senior Secretary-General again requested the heads of various external departments to come to the council to explain. (Hualian Dian [China Allied Press Telegram] on the 15th)

Gu Mengyu and Chen Gongbo Arrive in Shanghai to Welcome Wang Jingwei 18

Tang Youren Discusses the Current Situation

(Nanjing) Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu went to Shanghai at Shenke [3-5 PM] on the 15th, and Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo went to Shanghai on the night of the 14th, both to welcome Wang Jingwei. Other ministers will go to Shanghai on the evening of the 16th to meet with Wang, after which they will hold a conference in Shanghai to discuss major plans for resisting Japan and saving the nation. Whether Wang Jingwei will come to Nanjing immediately after arriving in Shanghai to resume his position as President of the Executive Yuan will reportedly be decided at this conference. The ministers are scheduled to return to Nanjing on the 18th. Tang Youren said that Wang could arrive on the morning of the 17th, and that Wang's anti-Japanese sentiment is very high, in line with his consistent stance in the past, but having been abroad for several months, it is of course necessary for him to first understand the situation within the country. Roughly speaking, the current problems facing China are: (1) Can the League of Nations sanction Japan? The League of Nations is not absolutely incapable of this, but it is conditional, that is, whether sanctioning Japan is beneficial to the League of Nations itself is the standard. The League of Nations will absolutely not sacrifice its own interests to aid China. Under these conditions, what will become of China? After the three northeastern provinces were not recovered, Rehe also fell. When has the League of Nations shown any determination to sanction Japan? (2) Japan's conditions for direct negotiations between China and Japan would likely exclude the issue of the three northeastern provinces and Rehe. However, what our country wants to negotiate is the recovery of lost territories. If the issue of lost territories cannot be negotiated, what else is there to discuss? If the powers sit idly by while Japan invades China, and China and Japan cannot negotiate to recover lost territories, the result will be that within Shanhaiguan, China is invaded by Japan's mad military force, while within Shanhaiguan, it is enveloped by the diplomatic policies of various countries. What goodwill is there to speak of in the entire world? (3) Given the circumstances of the resistance to the Japanese army's attack on Rehe, should a military agreement be signed with the Japanese army in order to preserve the provinces of Suiyuan and Chahar within Shanhaiguan, which have not yet been lost? This is tantamount to hoping that the enemy will release their grip when their knife is already at our throat. Regardless of whether signing an agreement is shameful, even if we endure the pain and accept it, how can we guarantee that Japan will not invade again in the future? Furthermore, after our country endures the pain, will it be able to recuperate and train in a state of temporary respite in order to strengthen itself and seize the opportunity to avenge its humiliation? (4) China is an ancient cultured nation with a history of over 5,000 years. Will it definitely not be destroyed by Japan? Having this mindset is a sign of corrupt thinking. (5) Should the military bear considerable responsibility for the failure to resist Japan? This is not the case. The country is the country of the people, and the military only bears responsibility for the front lines. The people of the country cannot abandon their responsibility either. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Europe is Now in Decline - MacDonald Stands Alone to Save Disarmament

Draft Disarmament Convention Published Today

Reuters dispatch, Geneva, 15th - British Prime Minister MacDonald will present the most complete and extensive plan for the Disarmament Conference tomorrow. This plan is a draft convention, including all forms of disarmament and the results already achieved by the Disarmament Conference, including the security issue. This convention is for a period of five years. As for the meeting between MacDonald and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, it has not yet been determined. It is estimated that the two prime ministers may meet in Rome on Saturday or Sunday.

Reuters dispatch, Geneva, 14th - After meeting with representatives of various countries here, British Prime Minister MacDonald is now considering the details of the Disarmament Convention. MacDonald wants to make these details as broad, complete, concrete, and non-abstract as possible within the realm of possibility. A British spokesman stated today that the adjournment of the Disarmament Conference is actually useless in the current European situation. Europe is currently in decline.

Contents of the Draft Disarmament Convention 73

(Havas) Geneva, 15th - The British delegation has refused to announce the contents of the draft Disarmament Convention drafted by MacDonald. MacDonald himself has never disclosed his proposed recommendations to anyone, but it is said that the draft convention is quite large, about 40 pages, and all issues related to disarmament are included in it. Regarding the security issue, the Pact of Paris and the declaration of "prohibition of resorting to force" are first included. Rumors that the MacDonald plan includes a section on the British, French, and Italian Treaty are inaccurate. Regarding the limitation and reduction of troop numbers, President Hoover's proposal will be adopted. Regarding war materials, the number of heavy artillery and tanks will be restricted, and military aircraft will be prohibited. As for whether civilian aircraft should be banned or internationalized, it is unknown. The period of validity of the Disarmament Convention will be five years. The British side does not hide the fact that this draft convention will be subject to fierce disputes and will probably require several weeks of discussion.

MacDonald to Go to Rome Tomorrow 74

Havas, London, 15th - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon may go to Rome this Saturday or Sunday to meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. There is also talk that German Chancellor Hitler will participate, but this has not yet been confirmed.

National News, Geneva, 15th - The fate of the Disarmament Conference may take a turn for the better at the Rome conference on Saturday, when British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon will meet with Mussolini in the Italian capital. There is also talk that German Chancellor Hitler will participate, but this has not yet been confirmed.

British Envoy Visits German Foreign Minister 75

Reuters, Berlin, 14th - British Ambassador to Germany, Rumbold, discussed the disarmament issue with the German Foreign Minister today. The German Foreign Minister stated that Germany's attitude has not changed. In other words, unless all countries disarm, Germany is free to adopt necessary plans to ensure its security.

Havas, Berlin, 14th - The German Nationalist Stock Exchange newspaper reported that Germany enjoys equal rights with all countries in terms of armaments and security. If the Disarmament Conference fails, the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles restricting German armaments will be invalid according to the principle of equality.

Borah Recommends Recognition of Soviet Russia in the US Senate 76

TASS, Washington, 14th - Senator Borah, a Republican from Idaho and a strong advocate for US recognition of the Soviet Union, made a recommendation in the Senate, arguing that the US government should take immediate steps to recognize the Soviet Union. After some discussion, the Senate handed the motion over to the Foreign Relations Committee.

Japan Relieves Agricultural Distress 77

Farmers Owe 450 Million Yuan

Reuters, Tokyo, 15th - During today's parliamentary debate on the farmers' debt repayment fund bill, it was discovered that Japanese farmers throughout the country owe a total of 450 million Japanese yen. It is now proposed to lend each farmer 1,000 yen to relieve them of their debt. The bill also recommends starting a debt repayment fund, initially setting it at 20 million yen and gradually increasing it to 200 million yen, to be lent out by the postal savings bureau.

Is Japan's Trade with Us Improving? 78

Reuters, Tokyo, 15th - According to a trade report released by the Ministry of Finance, trade with China, Manchuria, Hong Kong, and the Kwantung Leased Territory in February totaled 59,282,000 Japanese yen. In the same month last year, it was only 34,548,000 Japanese yen, indicating that there has been progress this year.

Page 11

National Panic in Japan 79

Major Cities and Industrial Centers

Feared Bombing by US and Russian Air Forces

Araki and Osumi Issue Proclamations to Reassure the People

Reuters, Tokyo, 15th - Recently, a nationwide panic has arisen in Japan, as Japan's major cities and manufacturing centers are feared to be flattened by bombs from aircraft. The panic has two causes: first, an article recently published in a certain magazine by a certain US admiral stated that the US air force could attack Japan via the Aleutian Islands, and this article has been translated and published in various Japanese newspapers; second, the Soviet Union has military air stations in Vladivostok and Khabarovsk, close to Japan. Therefore, Minister of the Army Araki and Minister of the Navy Osumi have issued proclamations to reassure the people. It is said that as a result of continuous efforts, the fighter planes currently manufactured in Japan, although not superior to those of foreign countries, are already on par. The army and navy have today's air force, which is sufficient to repel any aerial attack. Araki admitted that Japan's aviation knowledge still has regrets, but said that Japanese army soldiers are now receiving full aviation training. In addition, this year's budget has stipulated the organization of a youth aviation corps, in order to instill military aviation knowledge in the youth of the country. In recent months, the Japanese people have cooperated thoroughly with the army authorities in carrying out exercises to resist aerial attacks, so he dares to be sure that even if the enemy can attack from the sky, the Japanese people can also defend themselves on the ground. Minister of the Navy Osumi also mentioned the proposal to establish an aviation department, saying that the Japanese navy's actions on this matter are entirely dependent on the US Navy. After thorough research, the US government has abandoned the idea of establishing a separate aviation department, so the Japanese navy has also decided not to do so.

France and Germany Negotiate the Rhineland Issue 80

Hitler Party Stormtroopers Moved

Germany Believes it is Maintaining Domestic Security

National Society, Berlin, 14th - French Ambassador François-Poncet visited German Foreign Minister Neurath today and formally protested the occupation of the Gelder barracks by the German National Socialist Party Stormtroopers and the deployment of German National Socialist Party auxiliary police in the demilitarized zone, claiming that these actions violated Article 43 of the peace treaty. Neurath immediately rejected the protest, saying that the Gelder issue and the employment of auxiliary police were not within the scope of the treaty, because only one in ten of the National Socialist Party Stormtroopers currently living in the Gelder barracks carries a hunting rifle or a pistol, and even the auxiliary police cannot be regarded as a military force, so this movement is purely a matter of Germany internally maintaining local security. Havas, Berlin, 14th - French Ambassador to Germany, François-Poncet, visited German Foreign Minister Neurath today to protest the occupation of the Gelder barracks by Hitler's Stormtroopers, saying that the Gelder incident was not long after the Homberg Bridge incident, both of which were caused by Hitler's army, posing a danger of disturbing Franco-German relations. Regarding the legal issues, and whether Hitler's army occupying cities in the demilitarized zone conflicts with the Treaty of Versailles and subsequent treaties, François-Poncet temporarily reserved his opinion, saying that this incident not only shocked the French people, but also made all countries feel uneasy. German Foreign Minister Neurath recorded the protest and did not deny the misfortune of this matter, but said that the Gelder barracks were only temporarily occupied, and only one-tenth of Hitler's Stormtroopers were equipped with pistols or hunting rifles, so they could not be regarded as an army. Moreover, Hitler's Stormtroopers are only a political organization, and their trip to Gelder was only to maintain order due to the volatile situation. When the French ambassador spoke with the German Foreign Minister, he did not mention issues such as private armies being incorporated into the auxiliary police and whether this method complies with the treaty.

Reuters, London, 14th - British officials believe that the occupation of the cities of Gelder, Cologne, and Speyer by armed National Socialist Party Stormtroopers is part of Germany's domestic policy. If so, then the German violation of the provisions of the Treaty of Versailles that there should be no excessive activity in the non-garrisoned area is only a technical issue and not intentionally done by Germany.

He Yingqin Acts as Chairman of the Military Sub-Committee 81

Speaks to Employees, Encouraging Them to Work Hard

Significant Personnel Changes in the Military Sub-Committee

Martial Law Headquarters Established, Security Unlikely to Be a Concern

Beiping correspondence: After Zhang Xueliang, acting chairman of the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission, resigned, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has appointed He Yingqin to act in his position. He arrived at the Military Sub-Committee at 10:00 am today (the 12th) to take over the duties. The details are as follows:

This morning, He Yingqin, accompanied by Xie Zhongyuan, Liu Chuxiong, Wang Lun, Wang Guozhong, and others, guided by Chiang Po-cheng, took three cars from Jurentang to the Military Sub-Committee on Xi'an Street. A platoon of the garrison troops stood guard at the gate of the Military Sub-Committee, holding military bands to welcome them. The personnel of each department and office in the committee were all lined up in front of the chairman's office. He arrived at the sub-committee at 10:41 am. The standing committee members Wan Fulin and Zhang Zuoxiang had also arrived at the meeting. He then gave a speech to the staff in the courtyard, saying, "Today is the first time I have met with everyone, so I will make a few simple remarks. This committee and the Military Affairs Commission are one system. Because there are many troops stationed in North China, a sub-committee has been specially established to command the various troops. According to the organization of the Military Affairs Commission, the sub-committee is concurrently headed by the chairman. This time, Acting Chairman Zhang has left his post for recuperation due to environmental reasons. I, with the qualifications of Minister of Military Administration and Military Affairs Commission, have been ordered to temporarily take care of the sub-committee's affairs. I hope that everyone will continue to work and serve diligently, just as when Acting Chairman Zhang was in office. Do not be discouraged or lazy because of Zhang's temporary departure. There is very little time today. In the future, regarding the improvement of the army, you can make suggestions to me at any time, and I will adopt them separately." Then Wan Fulin spoke to the staff, saying that because the Deputy Commander is now away on business, everyone must follow the spirit of obeying the Deputy Commander to obey Minister He. At this time of national crisis, colleagues must work harder. After the third section chief Huang Shijing gave the salute command, He and Zhang Zuoxiang, Wan Fulin, Jiang Bocheng, and others entered the chairman's office to read official documents. He telegraphed Chairman Chiang to report the process of taking office and returned to Jurentang at 12:00 to rest.

He then gave a speech to the reporters, saying, "This time, I came north to inspect, but now, because Acting Chairman Zhang has resigned and left Beiping, the affairs here cannot be stopped for a day. I have followed the telegram order of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, in the name of Minister of Military Administration and Military Affairs Commissioner, to take over everything during Acting Chairman Zhang's absence, so as not to interrupt the duties. As for the organization and personnel of the sub-committee, they will remain the same as before, without any changes, and all affairs will proceed as usual. At this time of national crisis, I am worried and anxious. Although I am physically weak, I can only do my best to fulfill my responsibilities and work hard until Chairman Chiang comes north. In the past, political changes in China have often resulted in the successive changes of all the staff, so there is a saying that a new emperor has new courtiers. I am acting in this position, and the personnel will remain the same, and there will be no changes. As when I was in the Ministry of Military Administration's General Staff Department, I never lightly changed a single person. The Military Sub-Committee is a branch of the Military Affairs Commission, just like a branch store. Although they form two entities, they are actually a whole organization. The Chairman of Hebei Province is still Yu Xuezhong. Even if Wang Shuchang, the commander of the Pingjin Garrison, resigns, I will earnestly persuade him to stay. The security of Pingjin will still be the responsibility of the original chief officials, and there will be no danger. Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Shanxi, has met with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Shijiazhuang. I have not heard whether Feng Yuxiang will go there. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will temporarily reside in Shijiazhuang. When necessary, he may come to Beiping or return to Nanjing, depending on the needs of the situation. The front line of the war is still outside Gubeikou. The Central Army Guan Linzheng Division has arrived at the front line. The Central Government has a complete plan for resisting Japan."

After He took over the duties of the Military Sub-Committee, Ying Zhen, the Director of the Office of the Military Sub-Committee, has decided to resign. He believes that the position of Director of the Office is important and cannot be vacant for a long time, and has internally decided to appoint Chiang Po-cheng, a standing committee member of the Military Sub-Committee, to concurrently hold the position, but Chiang is still modest about this. Zhu Guangmu, the Deputy Director of the Office, has left Beiping with Zhang Xueliang. Chen Qinruo, the Director of the First Section, is acting as the Deputy Director of the Office. Tang Guozhen, the Deputy Director of the Third Section, has resigned, and He has appointed Gao Shengbao Yue to act as his replacement. The Intelligence Office of the Political Committee was abolished by order when Zhang Xueliang returned to Beiping from Dingzhou. All personnel were paid one month's salary. He believes that in this time of emergency, he has decided to set up another intelligence agency within the Military Sub-Committee.

As for the security of the city of Beiping, according to Bao Yulin, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, there is no problem with the security of the city. The rumor that the military and police requisitioned the bedding of residents is false. The Public Security Bureau has strictly ordered the district offices and teams to thoroughly investigate the source of the rumors. If such an incident occurs in the future, residents must hand over the evil-doers who requisition the bedding to the Public Security Bureau to be severely punished according to the law. In addition, because the front line war is in full swing, the order of the rear is extremely important. The Beiping authorities have specially established a Martial Law Headquarters, appointing Wang Shuchang as the Martial Law Commander and Bao Yulin and Shao Wenkai as the Deputy Commanders. Wang Shuchang also issued a proclamation to dispel rumors on the 12th, saying, "The situation is serious, and rumors are spreading everywhere. Inevitably, there will be unscrupulous elements who take the opportunity to cause trouble and try to disturb local security. From now on, if anyone is found harboring evil intentions, deliberately destroying or fabricating rumors, inciting the public, and all stray soldiers and vagrants disturbing order, and testing the law with their own bodies, they will be investigated and dealt with by military law. This commander has the responsibility to maintain security. All soldiers and civilians must strictly abide by this and not violate it in the slightest. This is the order." (12th)

Guan Linzheng Discusses Killing the Enemy 82

Wounded in Five Places During the Battle Outside Gubeikou

Doctors Say He Will Recover in a Week

Mr. Guan Says He Will Still Go to the Front Line to Fight

Beiping Correspondence: Division Commander Guan Linzheng, who fought against the enemy at the front line of Gubeikou, returned wounded on the 11th and is now staying in Xiehe Hospital. Today (the 12th), a reporter visited him and was led into the ward by a doctor. Division Commander Guan nodded with a smile to express his welcome. Although Division Commander Guan's complexion was slightly pale, his spirit was very good. After the reporter expressed his condolences, the doctor came to change his dressing, so he took the opportunity to observe his injuries and learned that Division Commander Guan had been injured in five places: one on the right chest, one on the left hand, one on the left thigh, and two on the right shin, all wounded by shrapnel. When changing the dressing, it was a bloody mess. The doctor predicted that the medicine would sting a little, but Division Commander Guan continued to talk and laugh during the medication, not thinking it was bitter. After the wrapping was completed, the reporter asked the doctor about the diagnosis. The doctor said that although there were many injuries, only one on the chest was serious. Fortunately, it did not injure the lungs. As long as the shrapnel is removed, there will be no worries. Fearing that it would fester, surgery is planned this afternoon or tomorrow morning to remove the shrapnel, and he will recover in about a week, because Mr. Guan's strong body is still sufficient to resist this injury. According to Division Commander Guan, "On the 26th of last month, I was ordered to kill the enemy. I arrived in Beijing that night and set off on the 28th. The entire division rejoiced and was excited. On the 4th of this month, we concentrated in Tongzhou and went to the front line of Gubeikou to reinforce the right flank. As soon as we arrived at the defensive area, we were only one or two li away from the enemy's front line. As soon as the war started, I led another regiment to occupy Longer Town to cover the right flank. Then we fought a fierce battle with the enemy. Our army used its strength to fight bravely. By evening, our army had recovered several small areas. The enemy suffered heavy casualties. At dawn on the 11th, the enemy attacked the right flank again with more than 10,000 people, and 21 airplanes dropped bombs fiercely. The artillery fire was even denser than rain. Our defense facilities were lacking. At 8 o'clock, two-thirds of our loyal and brave soldiers were killed or wounded, so they braved the bullets and artillery fire to fight the enemy in close combat. I then led a regiment to attack, and the enemy was defeated at first. At about 1 p.m., the enemy advanced to our first line of defense. Our regimental commander, Wu Yunbo, was killed at this time. At that time, the two armies were only a dozen paces away, so they fought hand-to-hand with grenades and bayonets. The sounds of killing shook the sky, and the blood shone in the eyes. The tragedy was so tragic that even ghosts and gods wept. I was hit by three bullets in a row and was finally wounded, but fortunately the soldiers obeyed orders. In past battles, they often took care of their own injuries and deaths, but now they went straight ahead without looking back. They were determined to sacrifice themselves, and both superiors and subordinates had the same idea. Therefore, although I was injured, it did not affect the position at all. Our position is still the same. If I recover in a week, I will still go to the front line to fight."

Division Commander Guan is from Shaanxi County and is now 28 years old. He graduated from the first class of Huangpu Military Academy and is a classmate of Division Commander Huang Jie, who is currently at the front line. Division Commander Guan also smiled and said to the reporter, "Why are there condolences for this minor injury? Moreover, the soldiers understand the great righteousness of defending against insults with spears. What is there to say about death? Injury is not worth mentioning. Although the enemy's weapons are very sophisticated, they are not as good as our soldiers in spirit and blood. As long as the people of the country continue to work hard, then recovering the lost land and striving for national freedom, in my opinion, is definitely possible." His words were extremely excited. Then the reporter bid farewell. Minister He happened to come to the hospital to express condolences to Division Commander Guan and expressed his encouragement to kill the enemy (12th).

Kunshan 84

Fire in Nandajie

At about 6 p.m. on the 14th, a fire broke out in the rear warehouse of Tongchangyi South Goods Store in Nandajie. At that time, a strong southeast wind was blowing, causing the fire to be out of control. Upon hearing the alarm, the fire brigades in various districts rushed to the scene to put out the fire. It took two hours to extinguish the fire. It is estimated that many warehouses were burned down, with a loss of more than 10,000 yuan.

The County Government Burned a Large Batch of Opium 85

The Kunshan County Government seized no less than hundreds of pieces of opium pipes, opium and red pills. At 2 p.m. yesterday, they were burned in front of the hall. The Civil Affairs Department and the High Court sent Taicang County Magistrate Zhao and Suzhou County Magistrate Zou to Kunshan to supervise.

Wuxi 86

A Large Batch of Red Pills Seized

Xu Bingsheng and Chen Jinhe, two people who have been selling red pills for a long time, hired a boat a few days ago and loaded 270,000 red pills. They sailed past Gaochang'an at dusk and docked. The villagers there saw that their behavior was suspicious, so several strong men boarded the boat to inquire. The boatman saw that the situation was not good, so he gave 70,000 red pills to the villagers as a gift. Afterwards, Chen Jinhe suddenly reported to the local drug investigation office, falsely saying that villagers in Gaochang'an were privately selling red pills and asked them to be arrested quickly. Director Chen signed and dispatched investigator Wang Julin, leading four guards, to rush to the scene. The 70,000 red pills were still placed on the shore. Wang immediately copied them and submitted them to the investigation office for verification, because the criminals who sold pills could not be found.

Land Survey Personnel Come to Wuxi to Survey 87

In order to carry out geodetic surveys, the Land Survey Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters specially dispatched survey personnel, carrying survey instruments, to survey the land in various counties. The survey has now reached the territory of this county, and reconnaissance marks, boundary stones, pile marks, and flags have been erected in various places in this county, all of which are the basis for the survey and shall not be moved or destroyed and must be permanently preserved. The bureau first sent a letter to the county government of this county to inform it and asked it to inform the districts, townships, and towns to protect it properly. After County Magistrate Chen approved the letter, he believed that the survey affairs were important, and all reconnaissance marks and boundary stones were the basis for the application of the survey and must not be moved or destroyed at will, or even slightly prevented. If there are trees that obstruct the area, the surveyors may consider cutting them down. In addition to ordering the local military police and district chiefs to protect them as important official duties, yesterday (15th) a notice was specially issued to inform the villagers that if anyone deliberately destroys the survey items or obstructs official duties, they will be investigated and punished according to the law and will never be tolerated.

Fire Kills Three People

Wang Xiaomao's family, a farmer in Dongwang, West Township, Xiaoshan, accidentally left a fire in the stove at midnight on the 12th, and Yun Shi burned four buildings and five bungalows. At least a thousand Japanese soldiers were killed every night. Up to now, the total number of prisoners and casualties is about 10,000. It is a victory that has never been seen before. The Hey Ming Chamber of Commerce Praises China's Progress 100

The Board of Directors Was Re-elected at the Annual Meeting the Day Before Yesterday

The Zilin News Reported That the Hey Ming Chamber of Commerce, Organized by Western Merchants in this Port, Held its Annual Meeting at Beike Yangxing Yesterday (14th). Chairman Mike Meijin Delivered a Speech, Briefly Saying That in this Autumn of Extreme Economic Recession, Everyone is Happy to Seek Signs of Future Progress. There are Two Things That I am Happy to Tell You: One is that Finance Minister Song Ziwen was able to solve a difficult problem that could not be achieved by human power, and balance the 21-year budget. The second is the efforts of the authorities in various provinces to build roads. In the face of unprecedented serious incidents, such as the suppression of the Communist army, the Yangtze River flood, the impact of the global economic downturn, and the hostile actions of the Japanese in Manchuria and Shanghai, the government's expenditures were huge and tax revenues were greatly reduced, but it was able to balance the budget. This can be said to be a miracle of financial management. However, although military expenditures have been severely cut, they are still the largest expenditure in the budget, accounting for 45% of the total. This heavy burden is completely unproductive and must be further reduced to a reasonable limit before it can be hoped that there will be surplus funds to supply more useful public undertakings. The Ministry of Finance's plan to reorganize domestic debt has been successfully demonstrated. At present, the market prices of various domestic debts have greatly increased. Although Likin and other domestic trade taxes have been abolished, the transit tax is still an obstacle to domestic trade. The road construction in various provinces is making great progress. We could hardly imagine the progress of today a few years ago, especially the progress in the past year. The authorities in various provinces have achieved such achievements in the most difficult period, which is gratifying. I believe that all of you wish their great plans to succeed everywhere. As for other conditions in China, it can only be said that the place is in a dark period. The Red bandits and other bandits are still not quelled, and national unity has not yet been fully realized. Although there are still signs of progress in many aspects, I sincerely hope that the current difficulties in the north can be resolved as soon as possible, so that various government agencies can have the opportunity to carry out their construction and reorganization plans to seek the welfare of the country. As for the commercial, shipping, and banking conditions in the past year, it can be said that they are in a dark age. The customs' tax report last year can be a clear proof. The average telegraphic transfer selling price in the past year was 1 tael of silver, which is equivalent to 1 shilling 8 pence 875 in British gold and 304 cents in US dollars. In the past, commercial practice used British exchange as a comparison. Since the UK abandoned the gold standard at the end of last year, this practice has been difficult to use. The impact of the global economic downturn was still slight in Shanghai a few months ago, but now we feel its true power. I believe that the most difficult period is undoubtedly ahead of us. However, if the country can maintain peace and the central government can represent the whole country, then I feel that the huge potential power of the market in this port and the extraordinary resilience of the people of this country will enable us to overcome the difficulties and rise from the abyss to the throne. In short, there are many hopes for the future. We must not be discouraged and disappointed. China and the world have repeatedly survived the same difficulties in the past. I firmly believe that the current difficulties can be eliminated at a considerable time. Then they passed the account summary for the past year and re-elected the board of directors. Mike Meijin was re-elected as the chairman, Buersen was appointed as the vice chairman, and Cokes and others were elected as directors. According to the previous Westerners' conferences, there were often many criticisms of Chinese politics. This time, only the two matters of finance and road construction were praised so much, which is also rare.

Visitors from Shantou Talk 101

Navigation is Prohibited for 14 Hours Every Night

Workers Unanimously Refuse Japanese Ships

Night Navigation Prohibited 102

A few days ago, rumors spread that mines had been laid in the Shantou port, prohibiting shipping and blockading the port. Yesterday morning, a reporter met a Chinese ship owner from Shantou to Shanghai and inquired. According to him, since the Japanese army launched the attack on Rehe, Chen Jitang has attached importance to the coastal defense of the southwest. Chen inspected the garrison in Shantou last Thursday and immediately ordered the Shantou coastal defense to be under martial law. Since that day, only civilian ships and merchant ships are allowed to enter and exit the Shantou port during the day, from 7:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m. These ten hours are the opening hours for navigation. After this prescribed time, traffic is prohibited. The prohibited hours are also prescribed to start at 5:00 p.m. and end at 7:00 a.m. the next day. These 14 hours are the prohibited hours for night navigation. Now ships arriving in Shantou mostly enter the port during the day, and mines have not been laid in the port, because ships can still sail freely. If mines are laid, the navy must lead the way.

Refusing Japanese Ships 103

In Shantou and Guangdong, the boycott of Japanese ships has recently intensified. Not only do workers at the wharves of Shantou and Guangdong refuse to unload cargo from Japanese ships when they arrive, but even sampans and small boats refuse to transport their crew members and passengers. Now, at the Guangzhou port, the section up to Bai'etan requires commercial vessels to use pilots to navigate into the Guangdong harbor. However, Cantonese pilots have unanimously refused to guide Japanese ships, making it impossible for Japanese vessels to enter Guangdong. It is reported that when Japanese ships arrive in Guangdong, their owners follow foreign vessels into the port and hire Taiwanese workers to load and unload goods.

Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, returned from Germany after recovering from his illness. Second Lottery Redemption of Jiangzhe Silk Industry Public Bonds Yesterday 111

A Total of Six Numbers Drawn

The second lottery redemption of the short-term public bonds of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry in the 21st year of the Republic of China was held by the Fund Management Committee at the Banking Association on Hong Kong Road at 10:00 AM yesterday. A total of six winning numbers were drawn, with a redemption amount of 180,000 yuan. The representatives present included Qin Runqing, Chairman of the Fund Management Committee (Supervisor); Wang Fang of the Audit Department; Shen Huachen of the Silk Cocoon Association; Chen of the Zhejiang Provincial Government; Shen Tianxin of the Zhejiang Cocoon Industry Association; Chu Huiseng of the Zhejiang Machine Manufacturers Association; Yan Shenyu, Magistrate of Shanghai County; Zhou Yuanxiang of the Jiangzhe Silk Wholesale Association (Lottery Drawer); Song Xunlun of the Zhejiang Local Bank; Yang Xuelai of the National Products Bank; Chen Huanqing of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; Li Yangsheng of the Central Bank; Shen Weiming of the Bank of China; Wei Tingtao of the Bank of Communications; Yang Chengyi of the Jiangsu Bank; and more than 30 representatives from the Qian Industry.

Chairman's Report 113

The meeting began promptly at 10:00 AM. Chairman Qin Runqing first reported, "Today is the date for the second lottery redemption of the short-term public bonds of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry. I am delighted that everyone has attended to witness the event. The short-term public bonds of the Jiangzhe Silk Industry were issued in the 21st year of the Republic of China, with a total amount of 3 million yuan. The first redemption was completed in December of last year. This is the second redemption, with six numbers drawn and a redemption amount of 180,000 yuan. All winning bonds will be paid starting from March 31st. The principal amount of the winning bonds will be paid by the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications branches in various locations, along with the interest on the bonds. Please ask the supervisors to verify the drawn numbers and the lottery register for execution."

Winning Numbers 114

After the report, the chairman appointed the lottery drawers to execute the lottery. As each number was drawn, it was presented to the chairman for verification and then handed over to the supervisors for double-checking to ensure accuracy. The winning numbers were then announced. A total of six numbers were drawn. The winning numbers are as follows: '06', '32', '58', '67', '76', '84'.

National Railway Product Exhibition Period 115

Around the 10th of Next Month for Three Weeks

Location Assumed to be the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society

Central News Agency reports: The National Railway Product Exhibition, organized by the Ministry of Railways, is actively collecting products in various locations. Yesterday, Xu Bingxiang, director of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Railways Product Exhibition, spoke with reporters about the preparations for the exhibition. Details are as follows:

Scope of Solicitation: According to Xu of the Ministry, this railway exhibition is being held to increase commercial freight transportation, improve railway operations, and promote domestic goods. The scope of exhibits is divided into raw materials, mechanical manufactured goods, chemical manufactured goods, handmade manufactured goods, artworks, mineral products, agricultural products, forestry products, aquatic products, hunting and animal husbandry products, medicines, patented products, and reference products. The exhibits are collected by the offices along the railway line and handed over to the Nanjing headquarters, which in turn hands them over to the Shanghai office.

Exhibition Date: Several thousand pieces of exhibits have already been transported to Shanghai, mostly industrial products. The exhibition date is expected to be around April 10th, lasting approximately three weeks. The location is the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Aimeiyu Road. It is expected that a large number of exhibits will arrive in the days leading up to the exhibition. According to the regulations of the Ministry of Railways, the exhibition will be held once every four months in different important cities. Therefore, after being held in Shanghai, it will be moved elsewhere.

To Establish a Display Hall: If the results of this exhibition are satisfactory, it is planned to select a location along the railway line to establish a display hall for permanent display of the various exhibits.

Anti-Japanese Generals from Heilongjiang, Xu Zihe and Others, to Return North Tomorrow 119

Various Circles Hold Farewell Banquets

Xu Zihe, Commander of the Fourth Army of the Heilongjiang Army, Cheng Yahe, Deputy Commander, Xu Qingshan, Garrison Commander, and others, arrived in Shanghai via Vladivostok and have been here for a week. Due to military affairs in Heilongjiang, they cannot be away from their duties for long and will depart north tomorrow. Various circles in Shanghai specially hosted banquets to bid them farewell. Details are as follows: Farewell Representatives: Various circles in Shanghai, in honor of the Heilongjiang anti-Japanese generals Xu Zihe and his wife, Cheng Yafeng, Xu Qingshan, and others, who are about to return north, specially hosted a farewell banquet at the Gongdelin Vegetable Restaurant on Parker Road yesterday morning. More than 50 people attended, including Wu Huanzhang, representative of Ma Zhanshan, as well as Huang Jingwan, Tan Bozhi, Feng Shaoshan, Xu Tongcong, Liu Renhang, Wu Lianghan, Qin Shaocheng, Xu Kecheng, Lang Jingshan, Ms. Bai Jingru (Huang's wife), and reporters from various newspapers.

Speeches by Huang and Wu: During the banquet, the host Huang Jingwan introduced the two army commanders, Xu Zihe and Cheng Yafeng, and reported the significance of the farewell, saying, "Today, we are hosting the true anti-Japanese heroes of Heilongjiang, who bravely kill the enemy, valiantly resist Japan, and selflessly defend the country. They are not like those who just spread slogans. The subordinates of the two army commanders, Xu and Cheng, number tens of thousands and are still stubbornly resisting in [missing text]. I hope that the patriotic compatriots in the rear will do their best to provide supplies and ammunition so that they can fiercely kill the powerful enemy." Next, Wu Lianghan gave a speech, saying, "The two army commanders are fighting hard on the front lines, while we are living comfortably in the concession. I personally propose that we retain them for three days and have various groups hold a grand farewell meeting to set an example for those who shrink back and do not resist." Finally, everyone raised a glass of tea to symbolize drinking the blood of the enemy.

Wu Huanzhang's Words: Next, Wu Huanzhang, representative of Ma Zhanshan, gave a speech, saying, "Today, Mr. Huang Jingwan initiated the farewell banquet for the two army commanders, Xu and Cheng, who are fighting hard in Heilongjiang. We know that they are the real anti-Japanese people. We hope that all circles will have fair criticism. I would like to report that General Ma Zhanshan is about to return. The generals are currently arranging things in the original place to prepare for a counterattack."

Cheng Yafeng's Talk: Next, Deputy Commander Cheng Yafeng said, "We came to Shanghai to pay our respects to everyone, but we did not have enough time to pay our respects to each of you, and we feel very sorry. Our work is not great. We must know the current situation of the Heilongjiang Volunteer Army. After the loss of Shenyang, there was no resistance for a long time. Later, General Ma Xiufang suddenly resisted. We think that the entire China cannot defend itself, but the small Heilongjiang is actually dealing with the Japanese. The provincial government was established in Hailun. We are willing to assist Chairman Ma and work on the front lines. Chairman Ma's position is also very difficult because Heilongjiang was also in the hands of the Japanese at that time, and the surveillance was very strict. He was not allowed to organize volunteer armies, otherwise the puppet state would disarm him. Therefore, Chairman Ma pretended to be accommodating to the Japanese while secretly investigating the powerful army in order to rise again. I (Cheng referring to himself) was unable to organize the volunteer army, so I went to other places to carry out activities and contact various troops. At that time, the Japanese side paid close attention, and the officials under the command of the puppet state opposed me and detained many followers, but most of them have now been released. When General Ma formally resisted, many people responded. We fought all the way to Nenjiang. The Japanese army attacked fiercely. Army Commander Xu injured both arms and lost his support. We still fought hard without retreating. After the Heilongjiang government was taken away by the Japanese army, the volunteer armies of all roads retreated, and the Fourth Army became an isolated army. The Japanese constantly sent people to persuade us to surrender. I told my subordinates that we would rather die than be humiliated. At that time, we were surrounded on all sides and it was very tight. I pretended to say to the Japanese commander, 'Now the encirclement is very tight, even if we surrender, there should be an opportunity to reorganize.' The Japanese army agreed to retreat a few miles and set a deadline of four weeks. I immediately led the team to retreat to the nearby mountains, collect supplies, and prepare for a counterattack. The local people transported supplies generously, but the amount of donations from various parties was very small. We have a total of 30,000 people. In the past year, we have only received 10,000 yuan in donations, so we can only defeat the Japanese to get bullets and food. Most of our soldiers wear straw shoes and thin clothes. Fortunately, the weather is still good in Nenjiang, otherwise at least two-thirds of the people will freeze to death. This time we came from Harbin. Along the way, the puppet state sent many military police to arrest us with pictures."

Impeachment Case of Zheng and Yang to be Handled by the Supreme Court 125

Designating the Jiangning District Prosecutor's Office to Conduct Investigation

If They Fail to Appear Again, Prosecution Will be Initiated

Since Zheng Yuxiu, the former President of the Shanghai Local Court, and Yang Zhaoyun, the President of the Shanghai District Court, were impeached by the Control Yuan for allegedly embezzling public funds, the judicial authorities have paid close attention to this case. However, outsiders have different opinions regarding the case's procedural details. According to inquiries made by the "New Voice News Agency" reporter stationed in Beijing to various groups, after the case occurred, the Control Yuan transferred it to the Central Public Officials Disciplinary Committee for handling. After several consultations, the committee members all believed that the circumstances were serious, and Zheng and others were not only derelict in their duties but also suspected of using their authority to embezzle public funds. If the evidence is conclusive, the matter cannot be concluded with a suspension from office. Therefore, the committee submitted a request to the Judicial Yuan, requesting a ruling. Judicial Yuan President Ju Zheng, for the sake of solemnity, and considering that Zheng and others had also served in important judicial positions, carefully considered the matter and decided to hand it over to the Supreme Court for handling. The President of the Supreme Court is also the President of the Judicial Yuan, so Ju Zheng, in his capacity as President of the Supreme Court, designated the Jiangning District Court Prosecutor's Office to conduct the investigation. Since the person involved in the case, Niu Fuchun, is currently employed in the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the Prosecutor's Office secretly ordered his arrest to investigate the matter. Although Zheng Yuxiu and others have gone overseas, a secret order for their arrest is also in progress. The Prosecutor's Office has already held one hearing and is preparing to initiate prosecution. In the future, the Supreme Court will need to designate a trial court, which will likely still be the Jiangning District Court; this is just a procedural matter. It is reported that if Zheng and others still refuse to appear in court, prosecution will be initiated directly after the investigation is concluded. It is said that the investigation work is progressing well and is expected to be completed within a month.

Lianxing Ship Runs Aground at Sheshan 126

Japanese Captain Unfamiliar with Waterway

The Lianxing vessel, belonging to the Zhaoxing Company, loaded with a large quantity of flour, departed yesterday morning from Shanghai to Yantai, Longkou, Dalian, and other ports. The captain, a Japanese named Tsūkawa, sailed the ship. In the afternoon, the vessel arrived at the sea area of Sheshan outside Wusongkou and, as usual, should have navigated outside Sheshan. However, the Japanese captain was unfamiliar with the waterway and took the wrong route, causing the vessel to run aground. For a time, it was impossible to dislodge the ship, and the hull was damaged. An urgent wireless message was sent for help. The coal transport vessel Taiping happened to be passing by and received the wireless distress call. It immediately sailed to the area two nautical miles east of Sheshan to assist in the rescue. At around six o'clock in the afternoon, the Zhaoxing Company also received an urgent telegram from the vessel and has already begun to arrange for a rescue ship. The extent of the damage to the vessel is not yet clear, but it is reported that none of the crew members or sailors were injured.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Submits a Request to the City Government to Correct the Customs Wharfage Dues Rate 130

Still Follow the 1931 Tariff

Collect 1%

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the City Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the request, the Sugar Trade Association wrote on the 14th of this month, 'Regarding your association's request to reduce wharfage dues, which was submitted to the City Government four times by this association, we received a reply from the City Government on the 8th of this month, stating: "All submissions have been noted. The wharfage dues rate collected by the Jianghai Customs was determined jointly by all parties. This wharfage due is now designated as a fund for city public bonds, and it is not appropriate to change it arbitrarily. Your request should be denied. You are hereby informed accordingly." The association has received this. We have investigated the agreement between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Jianghai Customs Taxation Department regarding the collection of wharfage dues. Article 1 states that it is collected at 1% of the imported goods, according to the 1931 import tariff. Therefore, there is clear basis for the collection rate. However, the Jianghai Customs is currently collecting 4%, and it is not collected according to the 1931 import tariff. This is inconsistent with the original agreement and should be corrected. Although the City Government has designated this wharfage due as a fund for city bonds and it is inconvenient to change it, the discrepancy between the collected amount and the agreement should be corrected. We hereby request your association to submit a request to the City Government to promptly instruct the Jianghai Customs to correct it in order to prevent arbitrary collection and alleviate the difficulties of merchants.' We have investigated the wharfage dues rate collected by the Customs, and it is true, as stated in your government's approval, that it was determined jointly by all parties. However, the agreed rate has already been included in the agreement, which states that it is collected at 1% according to the 1931 import tariff. If the Customs is collecting 4%, it is violating the agreement. The association's request for correction is precisely on this point, which is the same intention as your government's approval that it is inconvenient to change it. Since the wharfage dues agreement stipulates that it is collected at 1% according to the 1931 import tariff, the Customs should not collect less than 1% nor more than 1%. The association is only requesting that the agreement be followed, and it is even more clear that there is no intention to change it arbitrarily. Based on the foregoing, we hereby request your government to review and approve our repeated submissions and correct it in accordance with the agreement, which is for the benefit of the public."

Japanese Vessel "Fushimi Maru" Catches Fire En Route 132

Casualties Among Passengers

The Japanese Yusen Kaisha's European liner "Fushimi Maru" departed from Shanghai on March 28th, carrying passengers and cargo for Europe, first to Marseilles and then to London. On the 13th of this month, when it arrived in the Indian Ocean at 92 degrees 05 minutes East longitude and 6 degrees North latitude, a fire suddenly broke out in its fourth hold. Before long, the fire broke through the deck from the left side of the fourth hold and soon spread to the fifth hold. The wind at sea was strong, causing the fire to intensify. At one o'clock in the morning on the 14th, the captain gathered all the sailors and crew members to use the ship's special fire extinguishers to try their best to put out the fire. However, according to the captain's report, the fire in the fourth hold was very fierce from the beginning, so it quickly spread to the fifth hold. Some passengers in the hold were burned to death by the fire. Because the ship's hull was severely damaged, the company has ordered it to sail back.

Robbery Occurs on Shanghai-Hangzhou Train 134

At 10:05 yesterday morning, at the Shanghai South Station of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, just as the slow train for Hangzhou (third and fourth class) was about to depart, passengers in the third and fourth class carriages on the siding suddenly made a commotion, saying that there was a robbery in the carriage and shouting for help. The on-duty railway police officer, Cai Qingquan, hearing the alarm, bravely boarded the train and immediately sounded the police whistle. Police chief Zhang Cun and others also boarded the train one after another and jointly apprehended the robber and took him to the station. According to the robber's confession, his name is Li Guisheng, 32 years old, from Yexian, Shandong. Because he was unemployed, he wanted to go to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway to find a living. He had mixed onto the train twice, hoping to take the opportunity to rob passengers of their silver dollars, but he did not have the opportunity to do so. This morning, he mixed into the station again and entered the carriage. He saw a passenger carrying a large bag of silver dollars and, overcome by greed, disregarded everything and grabbed him to rob him. Unexpectedly, before he could snatch the money, the passenger shouted, the police arrived, and he was arrested. It is said that the passenger's name is Zhang Zhuoji, over 50 years old, from Jiading. He is the accountant of the new Datong Chinese Pharmacy on Heping Road in Ximen (West Gate). He was taking the train to Hangzhou this time to purchase materials from a glue factory with several hundred silver dollars. After questioning by the railway police station, he was sent to the local court for questioning with a written report.

A Pair of Lovebirds Arrested by Detectives

Publishing Industry 143

Scientific World, Issue 37. Scientific World, the scientific weekly founded by Wu Zhihui, editor-in-chief of the Greater China Science Research Society, has been published for thirty-seven issues since its resumption of publication. The editors are all well-known figures in the scientific community. It is distributed every Thursday with the Shanghai Morning Post. This year, due to the increasingly serious national crisis, the content pays special attention to scientific nation-building and materials related to national defense. This issue is published today. The main contents include Cai Yuanpei's scientific research, President of the National Central Research Institute; Xu Zhizhi's scientific movement; Wu Zhihui's source of national salvation strategies; Yang Yanju's introduction from ape to man; Liu Gui's national defense chemistry; Wang Ban's how to increase farmers' scientific knowledge; Li Xianwen's science museum in Yizheng; reader's corner; science correspondence, etc. In addition, the society has specially opened a science correspondence department, welcoming communications for discussion. Letters can be sent to the society at No. 280 Wangping Street, Shanghai.

A History of Chinese Political Strategies. A History of Chinese Political Strategies is written by Mr. Yu Chengzhi. This book is the only gateway to the study of political strategies. It lists 53 ways of using political tactics, all of which are explained in detail, explaining the methods of their application and change. The text is simple and the diagrams are clear. French Tram Fares Increased from Today 147

The Fourth District Branch of the Municipal Union Will Request a Stop.

The French tram lines have recently increased their fares with the approval of the French Municipal Council because of huge expenses, the low value of copper coins, and the inability to make ends meet. The new price list has been announced on all vehicles and will be implemented from today. The increase is one or two copper coins per ticket. Previously, the first-class fare ranged from 7 cents to 40 cents, and the second-class fare ranged from 5 cents to 24 cents. Now, the first-class fare is 8 cents to 42 cents, and the second-class fare is 6 cents to 27 cents. The above increases do not apply to the three tram lines, because they operate the same as the three Chinese tram lines, and the fares have not been increased.

According to Xinsheng News Agency, the Fourth District Branch of the Civil Union of the Second Special District will request the French Concession Taxpayers' Association to request the French Municipal Council to stop the French tram company's sudden increase in fares despite its annual surplus, in order to maintain the livelihood of the people.

The Little Hostage Kidnapped by Bandits in Taihu Lake Was Claimed Back Yesterday 148

Chen Zurong, the 14-year-old only son of Chen Tianyou, a wealthy man from Tangshan Baydi Village, Shaoxing Xiaoshan County, was kidnapped by Taihu bandits on the afternoon of the 19th day of the old lunar month this year. He was taken to Shanghai and hidden in the home of Chen Shiying, a Shaoxing native, in the third-floor pavilion room of No. 3, Ping'anfang, Lane 155, Xuehuali Road, French Concession. A letter was sent to the principal, demanding a ransom of 3,500 yuan for his release. It was agreed that the ransom would be negotiated at the entrance of Baoyuli, Caishi Street, French Concession, at 6-7 p.m. on the 9th of this month. The principal sent a representative to Shanghai. According to intelligence reports, the French police, led by Inspector Jin Jiulin of the Special Organ, and the Chinese and Western detectives, rushed to the negotiation site on time to wait. Twelve men and women, including bandits Shen Yun, Zhang Baichuan, Wang Achang, Lu Ruigao, Zhou Ruifu, Liu Xichen, Gao Bin, Chen Shiying, and women Chen Shengshi, Wang Chenshi, Wu Wangshi, and Fu Lanying, were arrested one after another, and the hostage was rescued and sent to the Second Special District Local Court for interrogation. Because the police found that the defendants had also committed crimes in Shanghai, they requested a postponement of the investigation. With the order to postpone the hearing to April 1, all the circumstances were recorded in the 12th issue of this newspaper. The hostage Chen Zurong was temporarily detained by the police, waiting for his family to claim him. Now, because the principal Chen Tianyou is ill at home, he entrusted his brother-in-law Ni Xuequan to represent him in Shanghai, submitting a request to the French police to claim the child. Therefore, the police yesterday escorted all the defendants and the hostage to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special Court for instructions. Judge Li Changnian took the seat. First, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen clarified the previous situation, followed by the principal's representative Ni Xuequan stating the reasons for claiming the child. The official ordered the victim Chen Zurong to come to the front of the case and asked about the kidnapping. According to him, at 6 pm on the 19th day of the first lunar month, I had just finished dinner when suddenly more than a dozen bandits came with guns and kidnapped me. That night, I walked with the bandits to the Qiantang River, crossed the river by boat to Hangzhou, and stayed in an inn for one night. The next morning, Zhang Baichuan, Wu Achang, Zhang Ruigao, and an unknown person took the train to Shanghai and lived in Chen Shiying's house in Ping'anfang for twenty-seven or eight days. After the statement, he also identified the faces of the bandits (who came to Shanghai and watched the hostage). The official then interrogated the defendants Zhang Baichuan, Wang Achang, and Lu Ruigao, who all confessed, saying, "We were hired by Mr. Shen. The four of us went to the principal's house together, pushed the door open, and kidnapped the child, holding two wooden guns and two flashlights. We first tied up more than ten men and women in the principal's house before taking the child out. According to Mr. Shen, we borrowed money from them because we didn't have the money to kidnap the child." When asked about Chen Shiying, he confessed, "Shen Yun, who is also on trial, used to be my colleague. He came to me on the 16th or 17th day of the first lunar month and said that a nephew was coming out to study business and would stay at my house temporarily. He promised to pay 10 yuan a month for food. Later, he said it was a kidnapping and sent the child on the 20th. Shen Yun confessed that he knew Mr. Shen, who invited me to Dayi Apartment on Bubo Road and asked me to kidnap someone, asking me to find a place to hide the hostage. I didn't agree. He threatened to kill my whole family, so I had no choice but to discuss with Chen Shiying to temporarily hide the child," and so on. At this point, the official announced that today was the day for the principal to claim the child. The child was interrogated in advance about the important parts of the case. The remaining defendants would be tried after the police completed the investigation. After the announcement, the child was handed over to his family representative Ni Xuequan in court. The defendants were still taken back to the police station by the detectives for detention.

A Gale Struck This City Yesterday 149

Since the beginning of spring, the weather in this city has been inconsistent with warm and cold temperatures. It has been raining and snowing frequently, not changing the winter climate. From the day before yesterday, it suddenly turned warm, and the temperature rose to about 60 degrees. Yesterday morning, it felt very warm. Unexpectedly, in the afternoon, the wind suddenly turned to a northwest wind, and the wind howled endlessly. The streets were filled with dust and sand. By evening, the wind was even stronger, so navigation was also hindered.
