Jiang Xiuzhen's Embezzlement Case Involves a Former Court Clerk 151

It is Said That There Were Matters Such As Using Badges to Intimidate and Defraud

The Trial Was Opened Yesterday and Further Witnesses Need to be Summoned for Investigation

Hong Baoming, the owner of Dehe Grocery Store in Fuzhou, reported that his accountant Jiang Xiuzhen had embezzled 9,300 yuan and fled to Shanghai with the money. He reported to the local Public Security Bureau and telegraphed to Shanghai, requesting assistance from various agencies to arrest her. Later, detectives from the Old Gate Police Station arrested Jiang in Room 8 of the Jiangsu Hotel and sent her to the First Special District Court. After several interrogations, because the place where the case occurred was in Fuzhou, the court ordered Jiang Xiuzhen to be handed over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for transfer to Fuzhou for trial. However, during the court hearing, Jiang Xiuzhen confessed that the case was orchestrated by Hong Baoming in collusion with Lin Fen (who had quit), a clerk from the First Special Court from Wenzhou, on January 31 this year, in Room 508 of the Central Hotel on Hubei Road, using intimidation to coerce a settlement, secretly using his official title, that is, the court badge, intending to defraud money, and filed a complaint against Lin with the court. The court approved the petition and issued a summons. At 3 pm yesterday, Prosecutor Guo Wei came to the Criminal Division 9 for investigation. The defendant, Lin Fen, complied with the summons and surrendered to the court. The lawyer Xiang Xun was also summoned to the court because he was a witness. First, Prosecutor Guo asked Lin, saying, "According to the complaint, you pretended to be an official in Room 504 of the Central Hotel on January 31, using intimidation to make Jiang Xiuzhen pay thousands of yuan to avoid litigation, otherwise you would have to ask the judge to sentence you to five or six years in prison, and you immediately took out the court badge to show that it was true. Is this true?" Lin replied, "There was no intimidation or false use of the badge. Because Hong Baoming is my nephew, Hong invited me to the Central Hotel to help with the settlement that day. I advised Hong to pay a certain amount of money so that this matter would not involve litigation, and there was nothing else. I reported to duty on December 1 last year and served as a clerk in the First Special Court until I resigned on January 28. The handover procedures were also completed. The badge was placed in the drawer of the office desk, but it was not returned." Mr. Guo asked again whether a tea servant Wang from the Accounting Department had asked you for the badge and you said that you would return it when you left. Lin replied no, and said that after he resigned, he temporarily lived with a friend in the South City, and went to Hangzhou on February 20, and returned to Shanghai on February 25, and left Shanghai to return to his hometown of Wenzhou on February 28. He returned to Shanghai on the 8th of this month and learned about this matter, so he entrusted lawyer Shen Yiqian to file a statement with the court to clarify the facts. He had indeed been to the Central Hotel for this matter, and lawyer Xiang Xun and witnesses Chen Xishun, Wang Yuqi, Ding Afang, and Shan were present at the time. Now, except for lawyer Xiang, the other witnesses are not in Shanghai, so they have not come to court," and so on. Then, lawyer Xiang proved, "I am Jiang Xiuzhen's agent. At that time, I tried to make the two parties settle, so on January 30, I opened a room in a certain room on the second floor of the Juelu Restaurant for negotiation, but it ended without results. The next day at noon, I received a phone call, asking me to go to the Central Hotel, saying that there was hope for a settlement, and asked me to go quickly to prepare a settlement agreement on their behalf.

I went there immediately, and Hong, Jiang, Lin, Chen, Ding, Shan, Wang, and other nine people were already there. Both parties were willing to settle, and Hong returned Jiang Yang's 3,800 yuan. I then made a settlement agreement and Hong Baoming wrote out the terms. Suddenly, Jiang took the note written by Hong and took the opportunity to leave, and his whereabouts are unknown, so the settlement was not completed and a lawsuit was filed. This is what happened at that time. However, I did see Lin Fen at the time, but there was no intimidation or removal of the court badge. If there was such a thing, then Jiang Xiuzhen must tell me, because I am Jiang's agent and must protect her according to the law," and so on. Prosecutor Guo Wei said that since some witnesses had not arrived, he ordered Lin Fen to pay a cash deposit for bail and change the date to seven days for further investigation.

A Bizarre Case of Seducing Young People 152

A Happy Encounter by a Character Analysis Stall

A Red Car Comes to Pick You Up

Large Qing Copper Coins as a Sign

The Police Lawyer Asks for Temporary Detention

Recently, among the unemployed and wandering people in the Zhejiang Road area, their long, disheveled hair has been cut into bald heads. The barbers' uniform actions towards these people have also been regarded as strange. Wu Chengen, a 22-year-old man from Ningbo, used to live at No. 348 Tiantong'an Road. After the Shanghai war, his house was burned and he became homeless and unemployed. He wandered the streets every day, living a wandering life. At about 8 am on the 7th of this month, while analyzing characters at a character analysis stall at the New Garbage Bridge, trying to predict when he would be able to turn bad luck into good fortune, suddenly a man claiming to be surnamed Wang came up and said, "If you want to find a job, now is a good opportunity. The Zhaofeng Chocolate Candy Factory at No. 24 Dengtuo Lane, Dengtuo Road, West Shanghai, is looking for workers and pays six yuan a week. Why don't you come with me?" Wu thought that a good opportunity had suddenly arrived, so he gladly went with him. Unexpectedly, the man said again that the workers recruited by the candy factory must not have beards on their faces or hair on their heads. They should quickly go to the barbershop to have their hair cut. Because he only had nine copper coins left in his pocket, Wang gave him eleven copper coins and ordered him to cut his hair. After it was finished, Wang said again, "I can't go with you. You can wait at the entrance of the Xianshi Company on Zhejiang Road. When a red car comes, I will call out the password 'Zhaofeng', then you can get into the car and go to the candy factory to get a pass and work." Wu followed his words and waited at the designated place. In less than half an hour, a red car came from the west, with license plate number 1285. Wang was also sitting in the car. At this time, Wu thought that the person he had met was acting strangely, and because it was cold and windy, he stood at the entrance of the alley across the road. When the red car came, he did not come forward to greet it. At this time, Mr. Wang, having not achieved his goal, also took the original car and went east. Wu thought that this matter must be

not good, so he went to the police station to report the above situation. The police station also had a Tang Rongzhang who had also encountered a similar bizarre experience in December last year and had already reported the situation, so he was immediately ordered that if he met him again, he could report to the police. Yesterday morning, Wu met this person again at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Xiamen Road and asked how the factory's recruitment was going. He replied that the factory was full and there was no way to do it, and gave him two small foreign coins as a travel expense. Wu immediately reported to the 1285 Chinese police, who arrested him and took him to the police station. According to his confession, his real name is Lu Wenbin, from Pudong, and he works as a tailor, residing at No. 53 Juxingli, Xinzha Road. A strange copper coin was also found on his body. This copper coin was transformed from a Daqing copper coin. One side was pressed with a very deep horizontal line by a machine, and the other side was pressed with a vertical line. Repeatedly viewed, it became a cross. According to what the police know, when the 128 incident was urgent last year, traitors often used this as a secret sign. At 9 am this morning, the police escorted Lu to the First District Court, where Judge Feng Shide presided over the trial. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the above case and said that Wu Chengen was poor and had nowhere to go. For the convenience of the interrogation, the police allowed him to stay at the police station last night and asked the court to ask him. Although Tang Rongzhang could not be present in court today, the police had a way to bring him to the case. In order to prove whether the defendant was a tailor, a detective was sent to the tailor shop on Xinzha Road to inquire. According to the reply of seven or eight tailors, they did not know each other. Only a woman upstairs said that he was her brother, because he usually made clothes upstairs, so the colleagues downstairs could not know each other. After Ru lawyer said that the defendant in this case seduced ignorant young people and the circumstances were bizarre, the police wanted to investigate the facts to determine which criminal law the defendant had committed and requested temporary detention. After Judge Feng asked Wu Chengen, Wu's confession was completely the same as the above. He ordered the date to be changed to one week for review.

Fictitious Company Fraudulently Obtains Guarantee Money 153

Chen Zigan's Intentions are Unpredictable

Arrested in a Hotel

Chen Zigan, a Sichuan native, who is already sixty-seven years old, falsely established the Tongyun Shipping Company at No. 46 Hankou Road in November last year, serving as the general manager himself. He advertised in various newspapers, soliciting staff and waiters to pay a guarantee deposit. A group of unemployed people went to seek employment. Mao Jiaogen and Yu Huajin, two Yong people, had been unemployed for a long time. Seeing the newspaper advertisement, they thought it was a rare opportunity, so they went to the Tongyun Company on November 12 and 15 last year and met with Chen, willing to work as waiters on the ship. Chen then ordered them to pay a guarantee deposit of 100 yuan each. Mao Yu immediately complied, and Chen issued a receipt, stating that the ship was now in Ningbo and would be able to serve one week after the ship arrived in port. Mao and others believed it to be true, took the receipt and left. After seven days, Mao and others prepared to serve, but Chen had already disappeared, and his whereabouts were unknown. Only then did they realize that they had been deceived. After searching around, they finally discovered that Chen was hiding in the Qinghua Hotel on Zhejiang Road, so they reported to the Old Gate Police Station, which sent Chinese detective Pang Yutang to arrest Chen and take him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Summary Court of the First Special District. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated the case, saying that the defendant was charged with fraud and obtaining property in violation of Article 363 of the Criminal Law. According to Mao Jiaogen's complaint, he also presented the receipt to the court. The defendant confessed that the Tongyun Shipping Company was not fictitious, and the ship had to stop temporarily because the machinery was damaged and required a repair fee of 3,000 yuan. He also hired lawyer Fan Gang to request bail. After Judge Wu Xiangzu reviewed the confession, since another victim, Yu Huajin, had not arrived today, he ordered the defendant Chen Zigan to pay 100 yuan in cash to be released on bail and change the date to next Saturday for further trial.

Reader's Advisor

Inheritance Issues 159

Letter from Si Yinjun of Zhenhai

Your newspaper's creation of the "Advisor" column allows readers to resolve all kinds of difficult problems. Every time I read the answers to the cases, I deeply admire them. Now I have an unresolved matter. There are five brothers in my family. We divided the property long ago. The eldest brother has three sons, the second brother has four sons, the third brother has no sons or daughters. The third brother died twenty years ago, and his ? is still alive. The fourth brother has one son, and the fifth brother has two sons. The third brother's wife, since her husband's death, has not adopted a nephew to inherit. According to what she has said to others: 1. She is afraid that the adopted son will be unfilial and add to her suffering in old age. 2. None of the nephews are outstanding or remarkable. If she randomly chooses one, the others will inevitably feel jealous and resentful. Therefore, she did not consider adopting an heir during her lifetime. In the future, after the death of the third brother's wife, rural women will not prepare a will or proper procedures. Inheritance will become a problem. According to the customs of our village, for example, if the eldest brother has no sons, the inheritance should be taken by the second brother. If the eldest brother himself prefers the third brother's son to inherit, it is called "love inheritance," and only half of the property can be given, while the other half must still be inherited by the second brother's son. Now I want to ask, since the third brother has no sons, the fourth brother should inherit, but the fourth brother also only has one son. Can one son inherit everything, or should the fifth brother be added to the list? I hope you will reply in a letter.

Answer: In today's social system, and in a Chinese society that has not yet escaped feudal customs, lawsuits over family property are truly endless. ? Your letter expresses your concern that the third brother has no sons and is unwilling to adopt a nephew, fearing that the division of property will become a problem after his wife's death. From our point of view, a person's property can be distributed to whomever they want, and others should not interfere. Even if the third brother has no sons, his wife should be inherited by his nephews after death. Only one person can be selected as heir from the room with the most nephews, such as the second or eldest room, and it is not necessarily inherited by the fourth room. Finally, we would also like to offer a sentence: "Good men do not eat the family's divided rice; good women do not wear clothes from their wedding." The meaning is that those who inherit the property of their ancestors are likely to fall into depravity due to food and clothing; those whose dowries are rich and whose families are wealthy cannot guarantee that they will not suffer for the rest of their lives. Good men and good women do not bother to pay attention to such things. If you are the so-called "fourth room," then we advise you not to fight for this unearned family property for your son. Winning a little family property may not be a good thing. If you have the ability, you should cultivate his education; if you don't have the ability, let him work. In the end, let him be independent and create his own path, which is the way to treat future generations. If you are the one son of the so-called fourth room, then you don't need to worry. Because we see that you are literate and eloquent and work in a public office, you should broaden your horizons. Why only ? at the family's small amount of property?

We pity you.

Concentrating the Strength of the Entire Soviet Educational Community

Purchasing the Jiangsu Airplane

Meeting of All Principals of Schools in Jiangsu and Other Regions

Six Measures Established for Examination Issues

(Jiangsu Correspondence) All principals of secondary schools in Jiangsu Province held their third general meeting at the Zhenjiang Normal School of Jiangsu Province yesterday (14th) morning at 9:00 AM in the meeting hall. A total of twenty-eight schools including Hai Shi attended. Tao Xuan chaired the meeting, and Cao ? recorded. The following important cases were resolved. Reporting Matters: (1) Examination outlines for all schools have been sent to the Education Department. (2) The normal school curriculum has been convened and agreed upon by the Xishi Luoshe Rural Teachers. Xishi has a written report. (3) The process of the Executive Committee held in Nanjing on January 10. (4) ? ? The current situation of the Audit Committee. Matters for Discussion: 1. Director Zhou is on official business. All matters of this meeting must be discussed with the director. Should we adjourn the meeting after the director returns? It was resolved to reserve it. 2. Examination Issues. A. Question of answering questions in science and English. It was resolved that Chinese and English should be used in the questions. B. Examination Grouping Issue. It was resolved not to group and not to test analytic geometry. C. Mathematics subjects for the examination. With algebra, solid geometry, and trigonometry as options, it was resolved to pass the options to the Education Department. The outline of algebra and geometry should be returned for re-drafting and sent to Nanzhong and Nannuzhong for review. D. Chinese language subject for the examination. It was resolved to allow both classical and vernacular Chinese styles, with three or four questions to be asked, from which students can choose to write one essay. E. Students who fail three or more subjects and are unwilling to repeat the grade may be issued a certificate of completion by the school and participate in the next examination after self-study next year. It was resolved to pass. F. For those with excellent results in the examination, the Education Department is requested to clearly stipulate reward measures and announce them in advance. It was resolved that: 1. The number of awards should be determined by the Education Department. 2. Issue scholarships. 3. Guarantee admission to university without entrance examination. 4. Issue certificates of merit. How should the subjects and class hours of the normal school curriculum that have been drafted be handled? It was resolved to recommend that the two schools of Zhen and Xi Teachers review it. Gather the strength of teachers and students from secondary schools throughout the province to donate money to purchase airplanes, and draft measures for public decision-making. It was resolved that: A. Concentrate the strength of the entire educational community in the province to purchase the Jiangsu Education Airplane. B. Measures: 1. Provincial secondary school students should donate at least one yuan per person. 2. Educational staff should donate at least 20% of one month's salary. 3. Suggest to the Shanghai Elementary School and the Elementary School Staff Union to accommodate the measures of this association. 4. Suggest to all provincial social education institutions and the Social Education Staff Union to accommodate the measures of this association. 5. From the end of April, all provincial educational institutions will collect the funds and deposit them in the local Bank of Communications and report to the Standing Committee. 6. Each union will elect two representatives to form the Jiangsu Education Airplane Purchase Committee.

Education Ministry Inspection of Social Education Personnel Returns to Beijing 163

The Ministry of Education previously dispatched Zhong Lingxiu, a section chief from the Social Affairs Department, to Jiangxi to observe social education. He has now returned to Beijing. According to reports, the social education facilities in Jiujiang include public education centers, libraries, and science museums. The social education facilities in Nanchang are even simpler. Zhong reported on the conference of public education experts, which resolved to promote the organization of public education institutions and the establishment of public education committees in provincial education departments, as well as in counties and cities, to serve as the central mechanism for promoting public education. He also discussed the allocation of 30% of newly added education funds in each province to social education expenditures, hoping that the province would strive to raise more funds to develop social education.

Additionally, Zhang Jiong, Director of the Social Education Department of the Ministry of Education, who was previously dispatched to Wuxi and other places to inspect social education, has completed his inspection. Zhang returned to the Ministry on the 14th and is currently compiling his inspection report.

Lehua Girls' Middle School Holds Board of Directors Meeting 165

Decision to Add Women's Supplementary Classes

Ministry of Education Continues to Announce

High and Junior Middle School Curriculum Standards (3)

Junior Middle School Physics and Chemistry

First, Objectives

(1) To enable students to understand common simple physical phenomena; (2) To cultivate students' habits of observing natural phenomena and arouse their interest in thinking about natural phenomena; (3) To enable students to practice using their senses and manual skills to improve their ability to utilize nature in their daily lives.

Second, Time Allocation

(1) Four hours per week in the fifth semester; (2) Three hours per week in the sixth semester.

Third, Textbook Outline

(The following textbook materials are the minimum required. The order of arrangement is for convenience of reference only and may be changed as appropriate during explanation.)

(1) Solids, liquids, and gases; (2) Length, area, and volume and their units; The convenience of the decimal system; (3) Weight and force; Unit of force; Specific gravity; (4) Chinese steelyard; (5) Buoyancy (e.g., ships and balloons); (6) Pressure within liquids; (7) Atmospheric pressure; Siphon; Gas pressure; (8) Air pump; Vacuum pump; and water pump; (9) Time and units; Clocks and watches; (10) Movement; Distance; Speed; Acceleration (e.g., racing and the movement of vehicles and ships); (11) Simple machines (e.g., levers, scissors, pliers, tongs, scales, pulleys, axles, inclined planes, screws, wedges, etc.); (12) Friction (e.g., skating, wheels, etc.); (13) Elasticity and strength of materials; (14) Vibration and waves; Water waves; Sound waves; (15) Loudness, pitch, and timbre of sound; (16) Scales and musical instruments (e.g., zither, flute, trumpet, bells, drums, etc.); (17) The sun and heat; Sources of heat; Friction fuel; and electricity; (18) Temperature and thermometer; Temperature scales; (19) Expansion and contraction of substances; (20) Heat quantity; (21) Changes of state; Ice; Water; Water vapor; Boiling and solidification; (22) Heat conductors and insulators; Convection and ventilation; (23) Rectilinear propagation of light; Shadows and eclipses of the sun and moon; Speed of light; (24) Reflection and refraction of light; Rainbow; (25) Plane mirror; (26) Glasses; Myopia; Focus and focal length; Erect image and inverted image; (27) Magnifying glass; Camera; Projector; Telescope; Microscope; (28) Sunlight and color; (29) Magnet; North pole and south pole; Compass; Geomagnetism; (30) Frictional electricity; Positive charge and negative charge; (31) Battery; Positive electrode and negative electrode; Dry cell and wet cell; (32) Electric current; Magnetic effect; Thermal effect; and chemical effect; (33) Conductors and insulators; Electric wires and fuses; Resistance; (34) Electric shock; Lightning; Electric shock (35)

Flashlight; Electric light; Telephone; Electric bell; Telegraph (36) Electric motor; Generator and electric motor; Electric fan; Tram

Fourth, Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Teaching Method Points

(1) The teaching materials should be centered on common sense and daily life, and should not be restricted by the organization of physics itself; (2) During explanation, the primary goal should be to enlighten students' understanding, and they should not be made to memorize mechanically; (3) The teaching materials must be made concrete so that they are close to students' daily lives. Phenomena that can only be seen in a physics laboratory should not be discussed; (4) During explanation, simple demonstrations and experiments must be performed to leave students with a deep impression of what they have seen; (5) Prepare more simple questions so that students can automatically seek their answers outside of class.

(2) Experimental Teaching Materials

(1) The use of compasses and rulers (e.g., dividing a wooden strip into equal degrees); (2) The use of triangles and protractors, and the method of drawing parallel lines; (3) Measurement of the volume and area of objects (determined by the amount of water displaced); (4) The relationship between the sides of a right triangle, and the value of π; (5) The structure and use of the Chinese steelyard; (6) The specific gravity of a regular solid (determined by its volume and weight); (7) The specific gravity of an irregular solid (determined by its volume and weight); (8) Buoyancy (determined by the weight lost by an object in a liquid); (9) Gas pressure, the lung pressure of the experimenter; (10) Pressure of liquids; (10)(1) Air pump and vacuum pump (drawings to show their structure); (10)(2) The use of pulleys (the difference between fixed pulleys and movable pulleys, and the combination of pulleys); (10)(3) Friction (comparing the magnitude of rolling friction and sliding friction); (10)(4) Strength of materials; (10)(5) Pitch of sound; (10)(6) The scaling method and structure of the thermometer (the difference between Celsius and Fahrenheit thermometers (10)(7) The use of a thermometer, body temperature, ice water temperature, boiling water temperature (10)(8) Heat, the temperature after mixing hot water and cold water) (10)(9) Expansion (the reason for the bursting of glass cups) (2)(10) Boiling (2)(10)(1) Pinhole camera, (2)(10)(2) Plane mirror (2)(10)(3) Myopia (2)(10)(4) Color of objects (2)(10)(5) Magnet and compass (2)(10)(6) Triboelectricity (2)(10)(7) Battery (2)(10)(8) Installation of electric lights and switches (common name: switch) Structure of (2)(10)(9) Fuse (3)(10) Electromagnet (3)(10)(1) Electroplating (3) In the laboratory, attention should be paid to the following points.

(1) Several sets of instruments should be prepared for each experiment to avoid the problem that the experiment cannot be connected to the lecture materials; (2) Students should be trained to make simple instruments themselves; (3) Students should be trained to make organized observations and records of common phenomena; (4) Students should understand the structure and purpose of simple machines; (5) Students should be trained to draw circles without the aid of circular drawing instruments to represent the structure of various simple machines, and to use compasses, triangles, and rulers to draw more complete drawings. 4. National Defense (Fortresses and important national defense raw materials of the army, navy, and air force) Lehua Girls' Middle School on Foch Road held its third board meeting at Yizhixiang yesterday. Sports 166

Jinan vs. British Navy

Courtesy and Respect in Friendly Exchange

Result: Four to One

Yesterday, the West Union Football Club had two Grade A matches. One was Yuyou vs. Agal at the baseball field, which ended in a 0-0 draw. The other was Jinan vs. the British Navy at Yiyuan, with Jinan winning 4-1. Several hundred people watched the battle at Yiyuan. Both sides showed courtesy and respect in their friendly exchange. Their performance was clear, pleasing, and commendable. Jinan's star player Luo Haiguang gave up football to participate in the Jiangnan University basketball tournament. However, Jinan still had the upper hand, with many scoring opportunities. Unfortunately, their strength was insufficient, and they were repeatedly saved. Nevertheless, they still managed to win 4-1.

First Half: Two to Zero. The navy kicked off at 3:00 PM and attacked first, repeatedly pressing Jinan's borders, but failed. National Games to be Held Around the Double Tenth Festival 173

Preparatory Committee Held First Meeting at the Ministry of Education Yesterday

Zhang Boling is the Chief Referee, Wang Zhengting is the Chairman of the Competition Committee

Participating Athletes Must be 18 Years Old for Males and 16 Years Old for Females

Women's Track and Field Events Added Softball Throw and Discus Throw

National Defense Scoring for Boxing, Wrestling, Weaponry, Archery, Pellet Firing, and Kicking

Other Competition Regulations Adopt the Regulations of the 20th National Games

(Nanjing, 15th) The Preparatory Committee for the National Games to be held in Beijing around the Double Tenth Festival this year held its first meeting at the Ministry of Education yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

Attending Committee Members 174

Attending Committee Members: Zhu Jiahao, Chu Minyi, Shen Siliang, Hao Gengsheng, Wang Zhengting, Zhang Zhijiang, Huang Liming, Zhang Huilan, Zhang Xinfu, Yuan Dunli, Ma Xun, Zhou Xiangxian (representing Ma Xun), Xia Guangyu, Zhang Jiong, Peng Baichuan, Xu Chonghou. Chairman: Zhu Jiahao. Recorder: Guo Lianfeng

Competition Regulations 3. Rules for Each Competition Item 4. Candidates for Chairman of the Jury, Committee Members, Heads of Each Group, and Section Chiefs 5. Notice to Attendees 6. Notice to Team Leaders and Oath 7. Notice to Athletes 8. Budget 9. Anthem 10. Receiving the Central Stadium 11. Temporary Proposals (6) Photography (7) Adjournment

Photography of the first meeting of the Preparatory Committee of the 22nd National Games (from right to left): "Front Row" Zhang Zhijiang, Wang Zhengting, Zhu Jiahao, Chu Minyi, Zhang Huilan, Huang Liming "Middle Row" Hao Gengsheng, Shen Siliang, Xia Guangyu, Ma Xun "Back Row" Xu Chonghou, Zhang Xinfu, Zhang Jiong "Rear Row" Yuan Dunli, Peng Baichuan, Guo Lianfeng (Photographed by Guanghua, Nanjing)

Chairman's Report

Chairman Zhu Jiahao briefly stated that the National Physical Education Implementation Plan decided by the National Physical Education Conference has been held separately by the central and local governments. After the National Games held in Hangzhou in 1919, it has awakened the attention of the national public to physical education. The National Government decided to convene the 20th National Games to promote the physical fitness of the people, but it was suspended due to the September 18th Incident. In this time of national crisis, if we want to revitalize the nation, there is no way to save the crisis without promoting the physical fitness of the public. After the European War, all countries paid great attention to physical education, believing that improving the physical strength of the people is an essential plan for strengthening the country. The National Games can awaken the patriotism of the national youth. Therefore, even though the situation is severe, the government is still actively proceeding in this difficult situation. Since the Hangzhou Games in 1919, the track and field records in various places have improved. It is regrettable that only one person from our country participated in the 10th World Games. The next World Games will be held in Berlin, and international preparations have already begun. All countries hope that our country will send personnel to participate. I have received invitation letters from foreign friends. In the future, I hope that all parties will work hard to increase the glory of the country. All the preparations for this year's Games will be under the guidance of you all.

Matters for Discussion

After the Chairman's report, Wang Zhengting and Yuan Dun asked whether the financial resources for holding the sports event were assured, given the serious anti-Japanese war. Were the costs of the provinces sending delegates to participate affected by the situation? After the discussion, Zhu, Chu, Xia and other department chiefs expressed that the committee will have the event as scheduled and the session was adjourned.

In the afternoon, Chu Minyi chaired the meeting and resolved the rules of procedure for the association, amending Article 4 to establish a competition committee, a jury, and eight groups: document, general affairs, accounting, propaganda, reception, transportation, security, and health. Two competition rules, the National Arts Championship were divided into Boxing, Wrestling, Weaponry, Archery Pellet and kicking, and women's track and field were added softball and discuses, with age limits set at 18 for men and 16 for women, and the remaining conditions would adopt amended versions of the regulations established for the 20th National Games. Thirdly, the item based rules were that the latest regulations were adopted for both women and men's basketball and baseball while other would be referred to standing committee to translate the regulations. Fourth, Chang Bo-Ling was appointed referee and a committee was established, with Wang Zhengting acting as chairman of the committee. Fifth, instructions to meeting attendants and group leaders as well as expenditure budgets were amended and passed. Sixth, the national games anthem was sent to all department and city schools for practice. Seventh, the central stadium was to be contacted by the group chairman. Eigth, a second meeting was scheduled to happen in May, to be called by the standing committee.

Regulations of the Shanghai Middle School Sports Association Basketball Championship (1) All teams are divided into "Shang" and "Hai" groups (decided by drawing lots by the committee). The referees' travel expenses are shared by both parties. (5) Competition venue: Borrowed from the China Basketball Hall. (6) Competition ball: Provided by the association. (7) If a team does not appear on the field for the stipulated competition time within ten minutes, it will be considered a forfeit. (8) The winning team must notify the chairman of the basketball association of each competition result within two days. (9) The list of players must be sent to the basketball chairman committee member Zhang Wugao (Xiaoximen Shanghai Middle School) before March 20th. (10) No school may request a rescheduling in order to end on schedule. (11) Except for the players, others must buy tickets to enter the venue. (12)

Spring and Autumn

Two Virtues in All Evils 178

— Zhan Lu

It is, after all, considerate of school children, from now on, school children can save part of their memory. Just because the most difficult thing for children to remember is geographical terms, especially when it comes to geographical problems in the provinces of North, East, and several others during exams. Now, the map of the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe has changed color... When children study geography textbooks, these four provinces can be skipped. Of course, it saves them a part of their memory, worthy of a call of considerate of school children.

It is, after all, considerate of student parents, from now on, student parents can save a part of their book expenses. Just because children's book expenses have been increasing recently; especially the picture books are more expensive than other textbooks. Now, the maps of the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe have been transferred to foreign maps; fathers and brothers buy maps of the Republic of China for their children, which can be reduced by four sides compared with the old maps, and the value is of course also reduced. It saves student parents' book expenses, worthy of a call of considerate of student parents. The non-resistance doctrine is all evils, losing territory and abandoning post and escaping is all evils; however, in all evils, there are also two virtues, that is, the two virtues mentioned above. Using virtue to resist evil is not all evils, it is only nine thousand nine hundred and ninety-eight evils.

Dripping Water 179

— Xian Xian

Buffer Zone

In our hometown, a lawsuit of "encroachment on dripping water" has recently occurred. Zhang Dage has one mu and three fen of land. On this one mu and three fen of land, there is a three-bay two-wing residential house. Wang Xiaosanzi, accumulating some hard-earned money, bought a piece of land next to Zhang Dage's, and for the sake of his descendants, he hired workers and prepared materials to build a small, low, and short bungalow. But Wang Xiaosanzi's short house built the eaves under Zhang Dage's eaves, so you say I encroached on the dripping water, and I also say you encroached on the dripping water. Everyone is unwilling to give in, and has to alarm the officials and go to court.

Logically, Zhang Dage's house was built first, and the rainwater from the eaves drips down. Dripping on his own land is originally none of other people's business. Wang Xiaosanzi's eaves drilled under Zhang Dage's eaves, it is difficult to say that it occupies the sky but not the land, after all, it is dripping water on other people's land. If Wang Xiaosanzi is a friend who does not speak crooked reason, he should have shrunk the eaves by one foot before building the house. Then, the water from your eaves drips on your land, and the water from my eaves drips on my land. Each drips the water from his own eaves, and no one encroaches on anyone, so this lawsuit can be avoided. But Wang Xiaosanzi is ultimately a poor man who suddenly became rich, unreasonable, and still wants Zhang Dage to demolish the house and let him.

This kind of "dripping water" is originally a very small piece of land, since they have become close neighbors, everyone should talk about a relationship. But the fact tells us that now people love "give an inch, take a mile." If Zhang Dage is easy to talk to, Wang Xiaosanzi will falsely accuse Zhang Dage of not only encroaching on the dripping water, but may also say that Zhang Dage's house is all built on his land, so he will pester you endlessly.

The Japanese have mentioned this kind of "dripping water" nature of the "buffer zone" in Shanghai and Jinzhou. Now I hear that they want to play this trick again between Beiping and the Great Wall. Everyone should pay attention.

A, B, C, D 180

— Juan Yun

The enemy is deep and the enemy is pressing! Occasionally talking to a friend about China's coastal defense, that friend smiled and said... "The four doors are wide open, singing an empty city strategy." Naturally, the enemy's warships can only charge and expand horizontally.

Perhaps those of us who have visited the Wusong fort after the Shanghai war have seen the ruins of those forts. From this destroyed fort, I was reminded of a joke about Zhang He, who built the fort, all his life. The forts along the Yangtze River estuary were mostly built by General Zhang He during the early years of Guangxu. This General Zhang was from Hunan, a leather worker by origin. After joining the army, he repeatedly made meritorious deeds and led some old Hunan troops. For a time, he was a brave and good fighter. He first served as the garrison commander of Huaiyang, and later was promoted to admiral of Quanzhou, Fujian. In the year of Jiashen in Guangxu, he returned to his hometown in glory and invited a group of local celebrities to a banquet. So everyone gave him a plaque, with the four big characters "A, B, C, D". Zhang He was a military man with no literary talent, so he hung the plaque high, thinking it was glorifying his ancestors and his family was prominent! Later, he talked to his staff in the office unintentionally. The staff then said... "Commander, you have been deceived. Think about what background you have? This A clearly looks like an awl, this B looks very much like a leather cutting knife, doesn't the C look like a board for cutting shoe soles, and the D is simply an iron plate for nailing shoes!" Zhang He was very disappointed when he heard this. He sent a letter home overnight and removed the plaque, so it was spread as a joke at that time.

Morning in Shanghai 181

— Zhu Shoujuan

A General Sketch

At the time of the faint dawn, there are no birds singing to disturb your good dreams here. Although there are occasional exceptions, there are intermittent chickens crowing from the small courtyard of the neighboring house; what we usually send into our ears is only a rustling of horses and a heavy whirring sound, then we know that the sun is about to shine on the earth again.

The trees on both sides of the road in the distance are shrouded in light smoke and fog, as if newly bathed girls wearing cicada wing gauze... In the vague and obscure, seeing its tender green new branches swaying in the wind, makes people feel an incredible emotion. A young village girl, with red cheeks and gasping, shoulders a load of fresh and tender vegetables and red radishes, taking hurried steps into this atmosphere. Before long, even her shadow disappeared, but the small calling voice of buying... scattered intermittently in the surrounding air.

The lights on the buses and trams back and forth have not been turned off. At this time, the passengers in the car are not the ladies in fancy dresses, not the modern youths, and not the enchanting women, because they are still lying in the soft and warm goose-feather quilt, seeking the most pleasant dreamland. They are only carrying children with schoolbags in their hands, housewives carrying baskets of vegetables, and people in plain clothes. Running forward, reaching their respective destinations, to do their duties in the daytime.

The sun gradually rises and falls again, and everything gradually changes; unfolding before our eyes is another picture.

Copper Coins 182

— Shi Yan Ye

A Hateful Thing

Copper coins, the ragged comrades who stretch out their hands on the street, sometimes may say thank you thousands of times to young masters and misses but still cannot inspire the other party's compassion and get one. For some people, they are regarded as extremely annoying things, and it is hateful to keep them and quick to discard them. Because its color is not beautiful, it is mostly heavy in quality, not as light as silver dollars and banknotes.

Miss Song bought a few small things at Sincere Company and got thirty or forty copper coins as change. Holding them in her hand, she felt filthy and heavy. Walking along the road, she hated them all the way, and finally secretly threw them away in a place where there were few pedestrians. Later, when I found out, I said to her; Miss! This is the best behavior of Shanghainese, but it is a pity that you secretly threw them in a place where there are few pedestrians. If you just threw them at the entrance of Sincere where there are many people, wouldn't it be more worthy of people's praise?

Two young masters of the Dong family went out to the suburbs to breathe some fresh air protected by a servant. In a small pond by the road, they saw two ducks following each other. The young master was overjoyed and dug out the copper coins in his bag and threw them one by one from a distance, meaning to drive them ashore. The ducks just wouldn't obey the order. You threw east, and they went west; you threw west, and they went east. After throwing a handful of copper coins, the second young master's bag was also thrown out. The servant's bag was also thrown out, but the ducks still didn't come up. He pouted and said; the copper coins have been thrown away, but they still won't come up.

Copper coins are indeed a hateful thing, I don't know why the ragged comrades on the street bitterly beg people for one.

Long Novel

The Fourth Company Commander of Northeast China 183

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Two 184

Simple Room Befriends a Wise Old Man in Secret, The Quan Family Chooses a Good Companion, Bitterly Condemns a Poor Child

Jiang stopped her and said; you are too busy doing this, do you need an iron now? The old girl said; isn't it easier to cut if the material is ironed flat? Jiang said; which excellent master taught you this, I have never heard anyone say this. The old girl heard it, had nothing to answer, but just lowered her head. Jiang didn't say anything more, looking at the Chinese numerals painted on the white wall, and asked; that pile of numerals is the size of the second master's clothes. The old girl said; the one on the pit, with two circles next to the numeral, is it. You don't need to measure, I remember it all, the height is three feet eight inches five, the waist is six inches eight, the sleeve length is two feet... saying, she raised her head and thought for a while, Jiang said... don't report them, I don't have that good memory, let me see one. So the mother and daughter hid in the house... and began to make clothes. The next morning, half of the clothes had been made. The old girl was afraid that the second master would wait for the clothes to wear, so she walked out of the door and planned to send a message to the second master, saying that it would be ready this afternoon. Just as she walked out of the door, she saw a carriage pulled to the door. Inside the carriage, there was an old man with white beard and hair, a fur robe and fur jacket, a hood on his head, a red face, and a pair of big eyes. Looking at him, he was full of spirit. The old girl was paying attention to this, and he had already opened the car door and walked out. Standing under the eaves, he looked up at the house number first, and then nodded twice and said; that's right, that's right, it's here. The old girl saw it, and it was clear that it must be the father of the Zhao company commander. They have already started moving in. She was thinking this, and the old man looked at her, cupped his hands and said; is this girl also living here? Only then did the old girl answer... Yes. Old man, your surname is Zhao, right? Company Commander Zhao came here yesterday, we talked for a long time. He is quite polite. The old man smiled and said; that's right, I am renting here to live. While talking, a soldier had already jumped off the carriage and was supervising the coachman to move the things on the car inside. The old girl saw the old man's situation, and she respected him very much in her heart, so she stood at the door and refused to move, just staring blankly. The old man followed the things in together, but he walked very quickly without turning his head, and went straight in. The old girl looked at it, and couldn't help but nodded a few times, indicating that this old man was good. (13)

Each Has Its Own Merits

A Groom's Account of Joining the Army (Part 2) 185

— West Lake Yilan

After a few more days like this; one day, just at dawn, hearing the groom's family, it was noisy again, crying and making a fuss. Those meddlesome people, in the coldness of the Hua family's winter heat meter three or five degrees below, weren't afraid, they put on clothes and shoes, and rushed to the lane. They only heard that the groom had run away again, and someone who had graduated from the army said; "It's not running away, it's joining the army." A Yangzhou nanny spat a big mouthful at the crowd, saying; "Chew the maggots of your granddad, the groom left early, are there two grooms? Why do you say he ran away?" The crowd was spat at by her, and they really felt that the rumors were wrong; but hearing is not as good as seeing, just as the groom's family opened the door, a few pioneers boldly went in; the crowd followed one after another, and filled a room. With so many people, they weren't afraid that the host would issue an eviction order. They only saw Many Stars crying and shouting, wanting the life of his grandson's wife; the groom's father and mother were also forcing the daughter-in-law, saying that she shouldn't have tricked my son into leaving. The bride saw that there were many people in the room, so she walked into the crowd and said in a loud voice; "You all are good neighbors, I am going to leave you today, I must tell you about our family affairs. My husband, I persuaded him to join the army last time. Because he originally studied military affairs, and now at home, his grandmother, his parents, teach him to eat and make feces at home, ruining a promising young man. Speaking of the current national crisis, all those who can do a little bit of effort should go to the front line! Do you know if China is gone, will there still be these people of us? If the land is gone, the country is gone, can we still eat stably at home! I persuaded my husband to join the army, although he is not brave now, but he was very moved when he heard my words, so he left by himself. Unexpectedly, after a few days, he secretly came back last night; his family was so happy, but I was extremely angry. He said... 'Many friends persuaded me not to go, and forcibly sent me back.' He also tried to please me, saying... 'He couldn't bear to leave me.' I broke up with him that night. I said... 'If you don't love the country, what do you love a wife! If you go to the front line and defeat the Japanese, you will be my husband; if you don't win, you still have a best future to go, which is death! If you come back without winning, you are not my husband! And I am not your wife! If you come back today and become a dull machine for eating and making feces, I will let you go. Even if you love me, I don't want this kind of shameless and cowardly husband.' He listened to my words, and he was really moved. He wanted to leave immediately, so I poured him a glass of wine and said... 'Please drink it dry, this glass of wine is our last glass of wine! If it doesn't count as the last one and we have to pour you another glass in the future, then our glory is also worth an indulgence.' The bride said this to the crowd, some understood, some didn't, but seeing her generous attitude, listening

She stopped and said again... 'I am pregnant now, and I can't go with my husband, but in another five months, I will also go to the front line to do my part.' She also said... 'As for the family here, they all hate me so much, I can't stay here any longer. I will go back to my mother's house immediately.' After she finished speaking, she strode away. Everyone followed her out of the lane, and didn't come back until they couldn't see her anymore.

I don't know what kind of magic she possessed, but so many people in the lane were deeply moved by her speech. Later, open-air meetings were still held every day; the things discussed at the meetings were always inseparable from her. Before, everyone called her the bride, but after her speech, she got another most dignified and glorious nickname, calling her "female hero."

Guidelines for Submitting to the National Products Weekly 186

(1) This magazine solicits the following manuscripts: (1) Investigation and research on national product factories and domestically produced raw materials; (2) Discussion on improving the production and sales of national products; (3) Records of lectures and talks on the national product community; (4) Introduction to new national product businesses; (5) Interviews with national product businesses and their leaders;

(6) National product news; (7) Other texts, photos, and illustrations about national products that are interesting and valuable.

(1) Manuscripts are not limited to style, but focus on conciseness and vividness, with each article limited to 500 words; those with special value should not exceed 1,000 words at most.

(1) Manuscripts must be written clearly and use new-style punctuation.

(1) The signature of the manuscript when published is at the author's discretion; but the author's real name and detailed address must be indicated at the end of the manuscript; and a seal must be affixed. (1) The editor has the right to modify the manuscript; those who do not care must be prepaid. (1) Manuscripts will not be returned regardless of whether they are published or retained; but this is not limited to those who have declared in advance and attached a stamped envelope. (1) Once a manuscript is published, a fee will be paid as appropriate.

(1) Please send manuscripts directly to the Editorial Department of the National Products Weekly of the Shenbao.
