National Products Forum

China National Products Company and the Chicago Exposition 188

— Yang Mang

The opening salvo of the National Products Year is the opening of the China National Products Company. According to the second salvo, the China National Products Company and the Chicago Exposition Product Coordination Association will hold an export exhibition at the China National Products Company in the Continental Department Store today. Gathering the elite of the country, collecting the special products of various provinces, and publicly exhibiting them on Nanjing Road, where there is a constant stream of people and vehicles, the significance of this is far-reaching, and the mission is important. It is worth proposing to the people of the country;

(1) The mission of the National Products Company is not only to widely sell products, but also to improve domestic products. The method of improvement lies in the exhibition, comparison by exhibition, competition by comparison, and progress by competition. This not only gives consumers a sense of feeling, but also producers can use this to encourage themselves. I have always been critical of Chinese national products, the biggest shortcoming is that they do not seek to improve, and have no vision for foreign trade. They are crude and shoddy, only seeking to sell well, and think that they have done their best. As a result, failures are everywhere. Very few are willing to use meticulous thinking, strive for excellence, to defeat foreign goods. The failure of foreign trade in recent years can be painful. This time, in the Chicago Exposition, the lacquer from Fujian, the pottery from Yixing, the porcelain from Jiangxi, the embroidery from Hunan, and the national products from various places, all feel that there has been a great improvement. I have studied the progress of products in the Nanyang Industrial Exposition, the Panama Fair, the China National Products Exhibition, and the West Lake Exposition. This time seems to be the most attentive, which shows that Chinese people have not made progress in manufacturing. Unfortunately, there are no scientific methods, no research spirit, and there are very few organizations in the society that are engaged in promoting and encouraging them, so the progress is not very obvious, and there is little propaganda power abroad, which is a pity. In the future, if any domestic product manufacturing can conduct this continuous research, and the industry will seek improvement day by day, then the scale of its achievements is immeasurable. This has to be hoped for the consistent efforts of the production community.

(2) Chinese people have always had a mentality that they cannot trust domestic goods, and only value imported goods, especially among the intellectual class and the propertied class. Now, look at the displays and sales items of this National Products Company and the Chicago Exposition. They are made with ingenuity and exquisite craftsmanship. Why are they inferior to foreigners, or even better? Then the Chinese people's self-contempt and self-doubt can be eliminated. Taking this opportunity, we can widely persuade them, fathers advise their sons, brothers encourage their younger brothers, and even husbands and wives, relatives, teachers and friends advise each other, to take the consistent use of domestic products as an honor and beauty. Then the development of the national product industry will be more and more prosperous, and the manufacturing can be more and more refined, and change with each passing day. The benefits of this exhibition to the national product industry are boundless. This has to be hoped for the consistent efforts of consumers.

The exhibition of the Chicago Exposition a few days ago was far away in West Shanghai, and there were very few visitors, and the distance was too far, which was a pity. Now, fortunately, it is being held at the China National Products Company on Nanjing Road. The location is convenient, and the time is appropriate. I know that visitors will be more enthusiastic and dedicated, so as not to let down the hard work and perseverance of the organizers.

University National Products Movement 189

— Gu Yuan

In the sixth issue of the Shen Bao National Products Weekly published on the 16th of last month, I had the pleasure of reading Mr. Pan Yangyao's article "The National Products Movement in the Family." He mentioned that "the consumption of foreign goods is mostly by intellectuals. The higher the level of education, the more vigorously they promote foreign goods, which can be said to be a matter of great concern." Based on what I have seen and heard, the author believes that the consumption of foreign goods in society is most prevalent among the intellectual class. What is especially worrying is the habit of university students to use foreign goods, so I specifically bring it up in the hope that those concerned will realize this.

Shanghai is a city with numerous universities, and there are tens of thousands of university students. They rely on the legacy of their ancestors to live comfortable lives. In a poor country like China, anyone who can enjoy a university education can be considered part of the intellectual class. When we examine the ability of the intellectual class to consume foreign goods on a daily basis, it is the university students who are the most formidable. This is an undeniable fact. University students wear leather shoes, use Stetson hats and Parisian hair tonic. These items have always accounted for huge numbers in our customs records. Although leather shoes made from domestic cowhide are slightly rougher in texture, they are far more durable than imported goods. Domestic hair pomades have also made significant progress in recent years, with good quality and low prices, but they are still not considered by university students. As for the clothes worn by university students, they are mostly imported Western-style clothes. Despite the good quality and low prices of domestic woolens from the Zhanghua Woolen Mill, they are not welcomed by university students who are dominated by the idea of "only wanting foreign goods, regardless of anything else." There are university students who wear Chinese clothes, but they are always in the minority. I have several friends who, after graduating from school and working in social service, enthusiastically participated in the national products movement, but they still wear imported Western-style clothes. When I jokingly asked them about it, they all said in unison that this was made while they were at school and that they would never have Western-style clothes made of foreign goods again. This shows how popular Western-style clothes are among university students. The fountain pens inserted in the pockets of university students used to be Waterman and Conklin, but now only Parker will do. As for Keds sneakers and cashmere sweaters, they are completely imported goods.

Sometimes I go to various universities to visit friends and see that nine out of ten things used by university students are foreign goods, which makes me feel deeply moved! This is only a manifestation of Westernization in terms of material things. When it comes to Westernization in spirit, it is even worse. University students like to mix English in their conversations, and amidst the noise, the tones of "Hello," "Mister," and "Miss" fill the air, as if they are afraid that Westernization will not come. This strange phenomenon can also be seen in the first-class carriages of trams passing through universities.

Analyzing the reasons why university students like to use foreign goods: First, they believe that foreign goods are exquisite and comfortable to use. After getting used to them, university students tend to buy them without thinking. Second, university students spend their time in classrooms, laboratories, and libraries all day long, and have little contact with the outside world. They have little understanding of the plight of a weak country and impoverished people. Third, the children who can attend aristocratic universities generally have some money at home, and university students have plenty of money, so they don't care about the high prices of foreign goods.

The bad habit of the intellectual class liking to use foreign goods is not limited to university students, but university students account for the largest number of people in the intellectual class. At the same time, university students are the future masters of our country. When we think that they have developed the bad habit of consuming foreign goods before becoming masters, the impact on the future of the country is unimaginable. Even in the present, there are no less than tens of thousands of university students in the country. What a significant impact these tens of thousands of loyal promoters of foreign goods have on the prospects of revitalizing national products! University students will occupy leading positions in the country in the future. Can we hope that they will have any thoughts of promoting national products when they themselves are stained with the bad habit of consuming foreign goods? The trend of the times will inevitably lead to all the financial resources of the country being sucked away by foreign merchants. Furthermore, since university students will occupy leading positions in society in the future, then the people under their leadership will definitely follow their example, and Westernization will become a trend. When wealth is exhausted and the country is destroyed, this will be the ultimate consequence.

What I have said above is completely based on objective facts. At the same time, we recognize the great mission that university students bear, so I specifically bring it up without any intention of criticism. At the beginning of this National Products Year, we have already heard enthusiastic expressions of support from many quarters. Now let us see how the universities, which are at the top of the national intellectual class, will rise up to influence and support it. We hope that university presidents, professors, and educators will advocate it from above, and that university students will implement it from below, creating a large-scale national products movement, leaving indelible memories and results for this National Products Year.

Introduction to New Industries

Introducing an Inventor 190

— Tianran

Mr. Zhang Wenping is a graduate of an agricultural university. He is very fond of research. Although his family is very poor, he has been tirelessly working on the invention of the sofa bed, which he successfully invented in 1931 and applied to the Ministry of Industry for a patent. In 1932, he also invented a rice transplanter and has also applied to the Ministry of Industry, but the Ministry has ordered that the machine be sent to the Ministry for testing within six months. Mr. Zhang is struggling financially and lacks the 1,000-odd yuan for the testing fee. He now expresses the following sacrifice: If any enthusiastic person can provide financial assistance for the testing of his rice transplanter, he is willing to transfer the invention rights of his sofa bed and grant priority shares in the rice transplanter after the testing is successfully approved by the Ministry. It is said that this machine can increase the speed of rice transplanting by thirty times compared to manual transplanting in our country. It does not use gasoline motors and can be operated by one person, which is equivalent to the labor of thirty people. This is also worth introducing. If there are any enthusiastic people, they may wish to cooperate with Mr. Zhang.

A Heady Admonition for Promoting National Products 191

— Ziqiang

Promoting national products does not require big fanfare and exaggerated advertisements with phrases like "big sale," "big discount," or "big sacrifice." You must know that in recent years, people have become impatient with cheap advertisements in various newspapers. If you still don't focus on practical matters and only talk about promotion, even if you speak eloquently, it's like a kind of anesthesia that cannot numb people's nerves.

The authenticity and affordability of national products have long been appropriately criticized in social discourse. There is no need to "prescribe a single remedy and sell fake medicine," nor is there a need to "hang a sheep's head and sell dog meat." It must be added that the so-called National Products Year is a period of national products revival. That kind of "deceiving oneself and others" and "creating something out of nothing" can be washed away with water. Only by restoring the original appearance will things improve. If national products are truly authentic and affordable, people will naturally come to your door. Otherwise, no matter how attractive you make them, you won't be able to attract these customers. In short, promoting national products can be summarized in the style of the Analects of Confucius: "If I am very good, what is there that people cannot tolerate? If I am not good, people will resist me, how can I resist others?"

A Battery Factory Worth Introducing 192

— Zudao

Although dry cell batteries are small items, according to customs statistics, the amount of foreign goods imported into China each year reaches more than 14 million yuan. How can we ignore this? In recent years, Chinese people have been able to manufacture them, but the capital is meager and the technology is not sophisticated. They are poorly made and the products are difficult to reach the top level. Moreover, the industry's vision is too short-sighted. They only know how to reduce prices in competition and do not know how to compete in terms of material quality. As a result, Chinese people are very dismissive of domestic batteries and the import of foreign goods has increased without decreasing. Now there is good news, and I would like to report it to readers in this bright spring of the National Products Year. My friends Ye Youcai, Yang Jichuan, Fang Yexian, Dai Renlai, and others are all well-known veterans in the field of national products. Seeing the downturn in the battery industry, they could not bear to watch foreign merchants plunder their rights and interests, so they raised funds to organize the Guohua Chemical Industry Company. They built their own factory at the intersection of Huade Road and Dalian Bay Road, hired chemical experts, selected the purest raw materials, and used the latest scientific methods to refine the Earth brand of various batteries. The quality is excellent and the performance is excellent. It can burn for sixteen hours and can be stored for more than a year. When I first heard their performance report, I seemed to be a little skeptical, so I took it to test it myself. Sure enough, I started guarding it at six o'clock after dinner and waited until twelve o'clock. Its clean white light was still the same as at the beginning, but I couldn't accompany it any longer. I went to bed, and when I got up at eight o'clock the next morning, there was still residual light, so I was sure that the performance of "burning for sixteen hours" was real. Later, I saw Earth brand batteries purchased a year ago in a friend's house, and they were still like new goods. This gave me powerful proof of "storage for more than a year." I am very happy, and now I have the opportunity to introduce it to readers, which is also a very gratifying thing.

Discussions on National Products

Charge Forward and Go Online Together 193

— Wan Gong

The bugle call for national products to save the country has been sounded! Kill! Kill! Kill! Let's all charge forward to the front line! At the same time, the enemy, foreign goods, is also desperately trying to break into our front line. In this tense situation, how should we plan our strategy to deal with the enemy?

The main force in saving the country with national products can be considered to be the several domestic factories in Shanghai. The China National Products Company is the vanguard of these main forces, and the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association is the headquarters. The organization of the National Products Salvation Army is probably like this.

Our first step, of course, should be to concentrate our forces and go to the front line together, but relying solely on the strength of the formal army is inevitably limited. In addition to the formal army (factories, companies, and associations), we should launch a high tide of national revolution, organize more voluntary soldiers (various national product promotion organizations), and sing the slogan "The whole nation unites to use national products" together to join the front line and fight a desperate battle with the enemy. Only then will there be hope of final victory. At the same time, the enemy has already copied our rear and is disturbing the rear. Look, in large and small cities in the interior, which place does not have the flag of the enemy (foreign goods)? "The enemy is deep, what can we do?" Our main force should also divide some troops to deal with him in order to save the oppressed masses in the interior. Otherwise, it will also end in a complete defeat on the front line. Also, almost all of the guns (mechanical production tools) used by our main force (factories) are the enemy's. Our war is becoming more and more tense every day, which means that their promotion is expanding more and more every day. In that case, before victory is achieved, we have already lost a key to be disheartened. Also, the symbols of our army (the decoration of national products) must be designed to be clearly different from the enemy's so that the masses can easily distinguish the faces of the enemy and us and make a unified attack. These two points should also be paid attention to.

Jehol has already been lost. Our (raised) army surrendered Jehol in vain without firing a single shot. If we want to save the crisis, we still have to rely on our national consciousness. Only by using the National Products Salvation Army to resist can we succeed. The bugle call for national products to save the country is blowing tighter and tighter on the front line. The headquarters, the main force, the volunteer army, and the entire nation must unite as one and shout the slogan "National Products Save the Country." Let's all charge forward to the front line together!

My Opinion on Establishing Mobile National Products Marketplaces 194

— Ai Wu

The primary meaning of promoting national products lies in seeking popularity. If you want to seek the popularity of national products, you should first enter the people's hearts and focus on towns and villages. Then mobile national products marketplaces or mobile national products exhibitions would be the best option. The method is to unite national product factories to organize them, select goods, pack them into boxes, and transport them to the interior. At the same time, cooperate with the public education hall to organize entertainment fairs, which complement the mobile national product marketplace. This is to attract customers. The first step is to go to places with convenient transportation first, spending ten days in each place before moving on. When a mobile national product marketplace is established in a certain village, hire workers to carry goods and spread them to the surrounding villages. The prosperity of the business can be foreseen. Moreover, this kind of mobile national product marketplace can use temples and other public places everywhere, which does not cost much, and the power of advertising is also very great. Those who are determined to promote national products may wish to try it.

Reading the Opening Declaration of the National Products Introduction Center 195

— Zhou Chengxun

National Products Year, National Products Year, a quarter of the year has passed in the blink of an eye. If someone wants to ask all the gentlemen who have dedicated themselves to the national products business: What kind of work have you done? Then I can be responsible for answering on your behalf. The establishment of the China National Products Company and the recent opening of the general office of the National Products Introduction Center are already the fruits planted by the hard work of all the gentlemen.

Without talking about the remarkable achievements of the China National Products Company in the past month, let us go on to read the opening declaration of the general office of the National Products Introduction Center. I remember that the declaration earnestly stated, "Engage in research on quality improvement, quantity increase, price balance, and market conditions." These few dozen words do indeed indicate the salvation and outlet for national products in the future. In general, national product factories that have a close relationship with the National Products Introduction Center should catch up quickly and jointly shoulder this important task.

To be honest, there are very few national products in front of us that can really compete with imported goods in terms of quality. Either the quality is simple and thin, or the work is sloppy. It is no wonder that compatriots are willing to spend the same price to find "goods from elsewhere." Anyway, the quality and patterns of some national product woolens can indeed rival foreign goods. The only fly in the ointment is that the prices are too expensive. It is impossible for us, the proletarian class, to ask about it. This is a matter of reducing costs for the factories, and I hope they will pay attention to it. As for quantity, it is even more pitiful to say. Often, a factory with short funds and limited output has to be monopolized by a local distributor. Large factories are also short of goods every day. Rootless trees and flourishing branches are everywhere. Moreover, competition among peers and year-round infighting, such as the rubber industry and enamel industry, have increased from three or four to dozens in recent years, and prices have been decreasing day by day. This is all due to business hatred, which is too unprofitable. They have completely forgotten the responsibility of developing products to the outside world, which is really heartbreaking.

The National Products Introduction Center has exposed these malpractices and pointed out a real path, which is revealed in the declaration. If you ignore it indifferently, go your own way, then it really contradicts the slogans of "promoting national products" and "saving the country with national products." You should abide by the words at the end of the declaration, "The same pace, the same goal, and everyone work hard from their own position," which is the most effective and practical work, and is a necessary step on the road to "production and sales cooperation."

I would like to present the above personal views to the advanced members of the national products community for consideration.

Introduction to National Products

Talking about Economical Oil Stoves 196

— Yong

Wonderful in that there is no smoke and no noise.

No need to pump air, no need for denatured alcohol.

Recently, a new domestic product has been invented in the market, called the "Economical Oil Stove." I bought one to try it out, and it is indeed good. The so-called "economical" is indeed worthy of the name, because its advantage is that the procedure for using it is simple. You only need to light it with a match, and you don't need to pump air or use denatured alcohol, like the trouble with pumping stoves. It is extremely fuel-efficient, and inferior oil is even better. It is said to use oxygen in the air as fuel, so the quality of the fuel oil does not matter. It only costs three taels of oil per hour, which is only sixty or seventy yuan. In terms of firepower, it is more intense than any other oil stove. The highest temperature can reach 600 degrees, and you can freely turn it down for low heat. Whether it is strong fire or low fire, there is no smoke or noise. Even if it is lit all night, there is no danger. It is really an economical necessity for the family. Now I will explain the advantages and usage pattern (see picture) of the stove as follows:

Advantages: (1) Economical in fuel consumption: Burning fuel oil uses air, so it is extremely fuel-efficient. It only costs three taels of fuel oil per hour. If you light a low fire all night for eight hours, it only costs three or four taels of fuel oil. (2) Quick procedure: Light it with a match, no need to pump air, no need for denatured alcohol, just light it with a match. (3) Safe to use: After lighting, it automatically gasifies the fire, so the flame is pure blue, smokeless, sooty, odorless, and noiseless. (4) Burning temperature: As high as 600 degrees or more, the lowest is about 100 degrees. (5) Convenient for cooking: Whether it is a round pot, a flat kettle, a pointed bottom wok, or an enamel cup, it can be placed on it. (6) Can be used for heating: In winter, add a heat shield on the stove to replace the charcoal stove.

Usage: (1) Unscrew the oil cap and add eight or nine tenths (about one catty) of fuel oil, then cover it again. (2) Take off the black lamp head and turn the lamp wick upwards enough to light it with a match, then put the lamp head back to its original position. (3) After one minute, it will automatically gasify and emit a blue flame, which can be used at will. (4) If you want to use a low fire, just gently turn down the lamp wick, and the flame will become smaller. (5) After using it, turn the lamp wick down enough, and the fire will go out. (Pattern see picture above) Note: (1) Do not burn all the fuel oil in the oil pot, otherwise the lamp wick will be damaged. (2) Do not cut the lamp wick evenly, the more hairy the better, the easier it is to ignite. (3) You can add oil at will while it is burning, it will not be extinguished. (4) When extinguishing, just turn the lamp wick down to the point where it cannot be turned, and it will naturally slowly extinguish. Do not blow it out, because blowing it out may prevent the emission of gas.

Contradictions 197

— Qia Yi Guan Zhu

The world is so big, there are endless contradictions to talk about. If you want to talk about them, I am afraid that this publication does not have so much valuable space to publish them. In desperation, then, I will first write out some of the strange phenomena of contradictions that I usually hear and see regarding the promotion of national products. Because, I feel that these strange phenomena of contradictions are not only obstacles to the future of promoting national products, but also a manifestation of inferior roots. If people from other countries see it, I don't know how they will ridicule it! Now I will cite two examples below, hoping that Chinese people will correct them if they have them, and encourage them if they don't.

Person A, young and handsome, wearing a Western suit and leather shoes, standing on the podium, talking eloquently. According to people who have heard him speak, he raised his voice and turned red in the face, all for the sake of persuading people to promote national products and resist foreign goods.

Persons A and B are in the same room, chatting about everything from national affairs to social anecdotes. Later, they talked about the market being flooded with foreign goods and no one paying attention to national products, which caused tens of millions of dollars to flow out every year, resulting in a weak country and impoverished people, and foreign insults coming. They sighed for a while and felt a little depressed, so A took out a cigarette case from his pocket, opened it, and first took out a cigarette for B. B took it and looked at it, and asked A, "What brand is this?" A carelessly replied, "This is 'Chesterfield.'" B listened and looked at A's cigarette case again, and asked, "Where did you buy your cigarette case?" A replied even more proudly, "I asked a friend to buy it abroad." B continued, "Then, when you have the opportunity, please ask him to buy one for me too." Qia Yi Guan Zhu commented: What I have said above seems to be two jokes. However, as long as we can pay attention to observation everywhere in ordinary times, strange phenomena of contradictions like this are not rare at all.

Scales and Claws of the Cement Company 198

— Wang Xiangliu

Reading the previous issue of He Koujun's masterpiece "Introduction to Domestic Cement" and the section on the Taihu Cement Company, the words were vague and there were still things that were not finished. Now, based on my own views, I have made a supplementary note. I wonder if He Kou thinks it is correct?

The Taihu Cement Company operated on a grand scale, hoping to produce 600,000 barrels a year. However, due to insufficient funds, the success fell short. The two smokestacks were already towering into the clouds, and the machines had just been set up, but they could not emit smoke, which was extremely regrettable. In 1926, the China Cement Company offered to buy it, and all the machines were transported to Longtan. A new factory was built next to the old site. As a result, the scale of the China Cement Company gradually expanded. At first, it only produced 500 to 600 barrels per day (which could be 300,000 per year), which was still second to Huashang (i.e., Shanghai Cement Company). Since the new machines went into production in 1929, it has jumped to become the second largest in the country, producing about 800,000 barrels per year.

National Product Inventor Fu Ji's Brief Biography of the Inventor of the Guangshi Spinning Machine 199

— Shen Youshi

Mr. Xing Guangshi, who makes people remember

On February 12th, the Shen Bao published that "Xing Guangshi, the inventor of the spinning machine, was commended by the government by explicit decree; and the Ministry of Finance was ordered to award him 10,000 yuan." From this, we can know that the government's encouragement of inventors is spare no effort. Now I will introduce Mr. Xing's story:

Mr. Xing, whose style name is Bu Wu, is from Haimen, Jiangsu. When he was young, he studied at the Shanghai Jincun Normal School and Technical School; he usually liked to study. When he was fourteen years old, he made a bicycle out of wood. After many improvements, he was actually able to ride it. Later, he imitated Zhu Geliang's wooden ox and flowing horse and created an iron ox that could carry things and move; but it still had to rely on human power, and it would tip over when it encountered uneven roads, making it very difficult to use. So he gave up and studied the earth's gravity engine. He used sixty-six gears, and it ran non-stop with gravity, but because one pound of gravity could only generate one pound of power, it could not save power in particular. So he changed his mind again; but he had already studied for six years, spent a lot of hard work, and exhausted most of his family property. Finally, he studied the spinning machine, because it was easy to succeed and could save the poor. He studied for seven years, and the eighty-spindle roving machine and the carding machine were finally completed. But it was not yet precise. Mr. Xing was originally very poor. He was able to concentrate on research for more than ten years, really because of his wife, Ms. Ni. At this time, he was extremely poor and had to stop. A year later, he was assisted by Huang Changding from Haimen, so that he could continue to build the iron seventy-spindle roving machine and the carding machine. A year later, the project was completed; who knew that when the assembly was about to be completed, Mr. Xing could not bear the torture of poverty and hardship and passed away. That was on October 20, 1929, when he was only forty-one years old. In the beginning of 1930, a foreign firm in Qingdao sent an employee surnamed Wu to Chongming to test the machine in Chongming. He offered 10,000 yuan to buy the machine, but Mr. Xing resolutely refused. He said, "This machine failed because it was not valued by the Chinese people. I will never give it to foreigners." From this, we can know Mr. Xing's fearless spirit, which is revealed everywhere, and he is truly worthy of being a successful person.

Mr. Xing was oppressed by the economy all his life, so he planned to set aside special funds when he was financially comfortable to establish a community to specialize in invention; but his ambition was not fulfilled and he passed away.

Can Chinese people consider organizing a community to help inventors like this who are in poverty?

Postscript by Ji Ping

Mr. Xing Guangshi worked hard to study machinery and invented the Guangshi spinning machine, which made a great contribution to the industry in our country. It is a pity that Mr. Xing could not bear the economic pressure and died from overwork. It is not only the engineering community that has lost a star. Two years ago, I was entrusted by Mr. Huang Changding to write a systematic account of this fact, which was published simultaneously in the Xinwen Bao, Shishi Xinbao, and Shibao of this newspaper, and was deeply praised by the Chinese people. At that time, Mr. Xing had already died, otherwise he would not have advocated public publication because he had not succeeded before his death. The Guangshi spinning machine is now being modified by the Engineering Research Institute of the Central Research Institute based on the principle, and it can be completely successful in about a year. It is not a small contribution to the textile industry in our country. This is not only the effort of Mr. Xing alone, but also the hard work of Mr. Huang Changding and the staff of the institute in planning, which is admirable.

Northern Gang Compete to Buy, Retail Investors Struggle to Cover

Twenty-Year Customs Duty Rises One Yuan Strongly

Yesterday, at the Chinese Securities Exchange, the market sentiment had already been reversed and was still rising due to short squeezes. The market price trend was very strong. The Northern Gang was the most eager to buy, and retail investors were particularly strong in covering shorts. In terms of the war, there had been progress. Large long positions were holding firm, and short-term swaps were more than long positions. The market price had a very prosperous outlook. The government's debt consolidation had reached 54 yuan. Some people in the market were looking at 57 yuan. Let's keep this saying for now and see what happens later. Various 20-year treasury bonds had all reached the 40-yuan mark. New high prices were found in various market prices. The strength of new buying was far less than the strength of short covering. Yesterday's rise was entirely due to the shorts' resistance, which made the market price rise higher and higher. Although the two sessions in the morning market were trending up, they were still stable. After the afternoon market opened, the Northern Gang had extremely strong demand, and all items advanced strongly. The market price increased by one yuan. However, the salt tax was relatively weak. Long-term government bonds, which had been silent for a long time in finance, had recently seen frequent ins and outs. Brown Sugar And Rock Candy 211

Cheap

Brown sugar is the raw material in sugar, and there are many types. What is said here is still produced in our country. Zhang Diaoqing is produced in Zhangzhou, and new ones are produced near the Winter Solstice. The color is yellow with red, and the sweetness is good. Those who are dry are the best. The sugar quality is rough, and there is a slight sand base (packaging method). The inner part is a wide bag, and the outer part is a hemp bag, or a double-wide bag. "Pu Diaoqing" is produced in Zhangpu, and new ones are produced near the Winter Solstice. The color is red with gray, and the sweetness is still good. The body is soft and has a sand base (packaging method). Same as above.

"Xinghua Qing" is produced in Xinghua. The goods are similar to Zhang Diao, but there are differences, somewhere between Pu and Zhang. (Packaging method) Same as above. "Chaoyang Qing" is produced in Chaoyang County. The highest quality is Tizhuang, which is delicate yellow in color and fine in texture. The body is dry, the sweetness is sufficient, and there is very little sand base. The next best is (Fengshan Qing), which is more delicate than Tizhuang Qing in color, softer in body, and has a slight sand base. The next best is (Huanggang Qing), which is inferior in color, dry in body, and has more sand base. The next best is (Longgang Qing), which is red, yellow, gray, and brown in color, still dry in body, and coarse in texture. The one between Huanggang and Longgang is (Bannan Qing), which is light yellow in color and without luster. The worst is (Sidu Qing), which is grayish-brown in color and has a heavy sand base, and the sweetness is inferior. In recent years, it has been rarely seen due to the fact that the goods are inferior and do not meet sales. (Packaging method) Double wide bags are tied with a single rattan.

"Jieyang Qing" is produced in Jieyang County. The color is as light as Bannan Qing, and the body is drier. The higher quality can be used as Tizhuang Qing. (Packaging method) Same as above.

"Chenghai Qing" is produced in Chenghai County. The color is light and tender, the taste is slightly salty, the body is soft, there is no sand base, and the sweetness is inferior. Packaging method) Same as above.

"Wen Qing" is produced in Guangdong. The color is red, the texture group sweetness is similar to Zhang Diao, the body is soft, there is no sand base, (packaging method) double wide bags are tied with double rattan

"Zhu Qing" is produced in Guangdong and is more common. The color is light yellow, the body is dry like Wen Qing, there is a slight sand base, and the sweetness is good. (Packaging method) Same as above.

"Guangxi Sliced Qing" is produced in Guangxi, and the best is produced in Nanning. It is shaped like a small inkstone and is a solid. The texture is thin, about three tenths of an inch. The color is delicate yellow, and the aroma is sweet. Locals use it to make tea, and it is regarded as a top grade. The one produced in Liuzhou is the next best. It is about four to five tenths of an inch thick, and the color and taste are slightly the same. (Packaging method) Wooden box.

"Guangdong Sliced Qing" is produced in Shiling, Guangdong, and is similar to the goods from Liuzhou. The one produced in Beihai is 0.6 to 0.7 tenths of an inch thick, the color is bright red and dull, and the taste is not very good, or it has a muddy base. (Packaging method) Boxes and barrels vary

"Brick Qing" is produced in Guangdong, shaped like a small brick, also known as sugar sticks, which is a solid texture, the color is red with black, the sweetness is inferior, and the resource base is heavy (packaging method) inner calculation outer package

"Ice Flower Qing" is produced in Zhangzhou, and is made from the remaining sugar brine after inheriting rock candy, so the sweetness is very sufficient, the color is yellow, and the body is dry. It is a top grade. (Packaging method) Single bag

In addition to white and red brown sugar, there is also rock candy

"Jian Bing" is also known as Wen Bing, and is produced in Zhangzhou. It is shaped like crystal and is a transparent solid texture. The color is white and slightly yellow, and the sweetness is very sufficient. High-quality goods such as Wufu brand white ice slices have the most and are not formed into slices, and the sugar pieces are less dross, light and unified hand goods. Conversely, (packaging method) the inner part is sealed with an iron box, and the outer part is a wooden box with fire, and then several sets or wide bags are added.

Free Talk

From Earnestness to Humor 221

— Five

Recently, some people have moved from discussing "humor" to "earnestness." I think that is not always the case. For example, on a tram, someone gets off, leaving an empty seat. Two good friends see it. Friend A invites Friend B to sit.

Friend B politely declines, "Please, you sit."

Someone nearby, probably misunderstanding, plops down in the seat, happily occupying it. The two friends can only blush and secretly complain. Courtesy and humility are undoubtedly matters of earnestness, but the outcome becomes a source of humor.

Foreign powers, under the guise of "international cooperation," partition China. This is done with due process and is undoubtedly a matter of earnestness. Yet, in the China being partitioned, some people actually send telegrams saying... this is "fair and just." Not only are they singing its praises, but they also drag 700,000 residents of Beijing to "express their condolences." Pity those 700,000 people; even if you halve it, 350,000 are asleep, with others using their names to beg for rewards.

Slaves praising their masters is, of course, a matter of earnestness, but dragging others to impersonate them to solicit rewards is truly the height of humor.

Asking warlords with vast wealth and concubines to defend the country is already unreasonable, and it is fitting that they do not want to resist. Yet, they still manage to issue earnest telegrams saying, "Even if it costs us a single gun or bullet, we are unwilling to lose an inch of land." And some people actually believe it earnestly,掏out their wallets to donate generously. The result of the donations is that the enemy is still far away, but the warlords have already rolled up their money bags, and for "strategic reasons, shortened the defense line," flee the scene. Telegrams declaring the determination to resist are earnest, generous donations are earnest, non-resistance is earnest, fleeing is still earnest. Only telegrams requesting dismissal and severe punishment, declarations, and resolutions are gradually entering the realm of humor. Yet, if it weren't for Ma Zhanshan's betrayal the previous year, a certain organization in Shanghai demanding the return of donations from him would still be considered "earnest." Yet, if it weren't for the general who created the non-resistance policy requesting the severe punishment of his subordinates for losing territory, it would still be considered earnest.

Using love letters to ask a lover to buy scented powder and silk stockings is earnest. Unexpectedly, a socialite in Guangzhou uses love letters to solicit donations and donates the entire amount to the volunteer army. Yet, when it comes to rescuing the country, there are no rules, and this is still considered earnest. It's just pitiful for those modern gentlemen who are filled with melancholy and unhappiness when they see national salvation donations. Now, their hopeful marriage proposals are preemptively tapped for national salvation money by their beloved sweetheart. They don't know if the beauty belongs to them or to someone else. They must be very worried, tossing and turning in their beds. Yet, proposing marriage, begging for love, and the rites of Zhou are all unquestionably earnest. A failed marriage proposal, pre-empted by national salvation, is what we call humor.

Therefore, everything is earnest first, and humor comes later. Humor comes from earnestness.

Therefore, articles about resisting Japan and saving the country, full of earnestness, are now only left with many humorous feelings.

Naturally, the fact that writing "inclines toward earnestness" poses the danger of spring's arrival and disaster's approach is not an insignificant reason either.

The Liberation of Ci Poetry 222

— Cao Juren

I want to talk about the story of the liberation of ci poetry. This story has nothing to do with Mr. Zeng's "special issue." Mr. Zeng sent me the "special issue," but I haven't read it. I'm also afraid Mr. Zeng will respond to Cao Juren.

The so-called liberation probably refers to the liberation of form and the liberation of consciousness. Ci poetry reached a certain degree of formal liberation in the mid-Northern Song Dynasty. Su Shi treated ci as a form of poetry, not limited to musical lyrics, and not wanting to be constrained by cutting and tailoring to fit the melodies. It was liberated from musical lyrics. By the Qing Dynasty, ci that could be sung had become a thing of the past. Many ci melodies were lost, and even those with melodies had unclear rhythms. The ci poetry of the Changzhou School could not be sung, nor could the ci poetry of the Zhejiang School. The trend was that ci was simply a form of poetry. In the early Northern Song Dynasty, ci poetry focused solely on the themes of sorrow and separation between men and women. Since Su Dongpo, ci poetry could be used to praise history, lament the past, discuss reason, and talk about Zen. It also underwent a certain degree of liberation in terms of consciousness. Xin Qiji, a ci poet of the Southern Song Dynasty, was filled with grief and intense emotions, and his themes were even more diverse. The Zhejiang School of the Qing Dynasty admired elegance and rejected licentiousness. The Changzhou School focused on intent, which was also similar to the consciousness of the Song Dynasty. Now, if we were to say that we were retreating from the diverse themes of the Song Dynasty to the focus on beautiful clothing and fragrances of the Five Dynasties, and retreating from the passionate and vehement spirit of the Song Dynasty to the "darling I love you" of the Five Dynasties, and then calling this liberation, wouldn't that be going backwards instead of forwards? If we were to say that treating ci as a form of poetry, not confined by rhythm and melody, is what we call liberation, then where would that leave the people of the Song Dynasty?

As far as I know, this girl who had bound feet was fashionable for a while after she unbound them. Later, she grew old and died, and was buried in Jiangnan. Now, her grave is covered with trees. Even if Zeng Genius wants to resurrect her, it would be difficult to bring the withered bones back to life. I think it's better to let her rest in peace and not make so much fuss.

Random Parisian Notes 223

— Xiao Shiyan, from Paris

(4) Edgar Allan Poe and Parisian Snowy Nights

At 9 p.m. on the 26th of last month, there was a public lecture at the Faculty of Arts of the University of Paris on the American poet Edgar Allan Poe. The lecturer was Professor Cestre of American Literature at the Faculty of Arts of the University of Paris. Despite the snow that night, many people attended the lecture. Professor Cestre spoke fluent French, and it was difficult for listeners to tell that he was American. He first briefly described Poe's life and masterpieces, and then discussed Poe's influence on Baudelaire. Finally, he mentioned that some aspects of France's most famous poet, Valéry, were also influenced by Poe. After the lecture, a French lady translated and read several of Poe's masterpieces. Her voice was very clear and loud, eliciting applause from the entire audience. The meeting ended near midnight, but the audience did not feel tired at all, and they all praised it as a very satisfactory lecture. Poe's life and "The Raven," which is called the American national poem, have been introduced by many people in China, so I don't need to repeat them here. What I want to briefly describe is Poe's theory of poetry: "Literature carries the Tao." This is not unique to China since ancient times; the same is true in Europe and America. This kind of concept of punishing evil and promoting good is probably based on humanity's sense of righteousness. However, when used in a very narrow sense, it hinders the development of the human soul. In the past, European and American critics always liked to find religious or moral components in a poem, as if poetry was only written for spreading religion or promoting morality. Poe ridiculed that Americans could not get rid of this kind of vulgarity. In his book "The Essence of Poetry," he put forward his views on poetry. He divided the activities of the human soul into three parts: intelligence, taste, and moral concepts. Intelligence seeks truth, moral concepts fulfill goodness, and taste pursues beauty. What is most valuable at the moment is sentiment, that is, a kind of yearning for beauty. In the moment of intoxication, the poet can feel the most sublime and eternal things that have not yet been understood by the world. However, the extremely intoxicated state of mind that a person possesses is, physiologically, only temporary and cannot last for long. Therefore, he said that the purest lyric poetry is only the shortest moment, not a long time. He used Milton's "Paradise Lost" as an example, saying that the most touching parts are only countless short poems linked together. In many other places, reading it inevitably makes people feel tired. He also said that the era of poetry singing the praises of morality and truth has passed. Poetry should have its own path to follow. Poe's arguments are the most modern, so his influence on the English and French literary worlds is extremely great. Some people regard Poe as the father of Baudelaire, saying that Poe's greatest creation is not his novels, not his poems, and not his criticism, but Baudelaire. Needless to say, Baudelaire is also called the father of the modern French poetry scene. From this, we can know Poe's position in the modern European and American poetry scene.

The Story of the Black Girl Seeking God (29) 224

— Written by Bernard Shaw, Translated by Yi Xian

Then she put Norbury out of her head, and went in and did the garden work with him. By and by others came in to help; at first this made the black girl jealous; but she hated that feeling, and before long she did not mind their coming and going.

One day she found a red-headed Irishman operating in the back garden where they grew vegetables.

"Who let you in here?" she said.

"Well, I let myself in, to be honest," said the Irishman. "Why shouldn't I come in?"

"This is the old gentleman's garden," said the black girl.

"I'm a Socialist," said the Irishman. "I don't allow any man to own a garden. That old codger's too feeble to do a hand's turn: he wants people to dig his vegetables for him; and there's more in vegetables than he'll find out digging them, from the time he starts to the time he's done."

"Then you aren't looking for God?" said the black girl.

"Not looking for God," said the Irishman. "If God wants me, he'll come looking for me. And I'm blest if He's any such thing as they say He is. He ain't properly made that way. There's a something pursuing Him in the world outside: that's what's the matter with us; and there's a something pursuing Him in the world inside; and that's the other thing that's the matter. Only one thing is certain; and that is that when the something is doing its best to get there, it makes a mortal lot of mistakes. And we—you and me—must do our best to show it the way; for there's a terrible lot of people thinking of nothing but their own bellies." With that, he spat on his hands and went on digging.

The black girl and the old gentleman both thought the Irishman a perfect brute (and so he was); but because he was useful, and would not go away, they tried to teach him good habits, and make him civil in his language. But it was no use. To get him to believe that God was something solider and more satisfactory than a Will that was not yet done might have been accomplished, even if it was not so easy to make that accomplishment seem reasonable and hopeful as Socialism made it.

Letters to the Editor 225

Letter from Mr. Hu Huai Li

To Mr. Li Liewen, Editor of Free Talk: I have read the article "Why Liberate?" in the March 10th issue of Free Talk, which was originally written in response to Mr. Zeng Jinke's "Liberation of Ci Poetry." Whether what was said is reasonable or not, Mr. Zeng himself will answer, and I do not need to participate. However, when discussing the issue of "Liberation of Ci Poetry," why suddenly involve "a gentleman who discovered that Mo Di was Indian?" And irresponsibly say, "He made many investigations in a grandiose manner." Since my so-called "Mo Di problem" is involved, I must speak. Now, I believe the author's words are incorrect and require correction and apology. The following is a brief explanation:

(1) If the author of this article does not agree with my statement that "Mo Di was Indian," then he should discuss it in detail based on my original book "A Study of Mo Di." And I should also be allowed to fully reply in the same publication. The author's first step is wrong. He simply said, "He made investigations in a grandiose manner..." and arbitrarily ridiculed it in the newspaper without reason. I believe this damages my personal reputation and must demand correction and apology.

(2) If the author still wants to discuss it with me in the future, he may also publish his opinions in Free Talk. But he must abide by two principles: (1) What he says must be reasonable, and both parties must not engage in scolding or ridicule. (2) He must allow me to fully reply in Free Talk. If this can be done, it may be followed. If it cannot be done, please publish this letter and automatically make corrections and apologize.

(3) If you, sir, do not publish this letter of mine, then I can only spend money to publish an advertisement in Shenbao. This will not be rejected, right?

Sincerely, Hu Huaichen, March 10th

Mr. Xuan's Reply

To Mr. Huai Chen: My memory is very bad. I have forgotten the name of the gentleman who discovered that Mo Di was Indian. Now I know it is you, sir, with all due respect! In my article "Why Liberate?" there is indeed the phrase "He made many investigations in a grandiose manner." But the so-called "made investigations in a grandiose manner" refers to your attitude when making investigations (and I must also say that your letter to Mr. Liewen is also the same attitude). It is not "irresponsible and arbitrary ridicule"! However, you may again take out the home-keeping skills of investigating "Mo Di's nationality" to "investigate" "making investigations in a grandiose manner," then I cannot bear it, and the small space of Free Talk is not the place for you to show your skills. So, I admit that it is ridicule and apologize first.

Secondly, I learned that you have a book called "A Study of Mo Di," in which you collected articles for and against the issue of Mo Di's nationality, following the example of Gu Jiegang's History Office. Just now, a friend found this book in a dusty pile of broken books and showed it to me. After reading it repeatedly, I suddenly realized the truth and felt sorry for you and sighed for the academic world. Why feel sorry? Because the gentlemen who severely refuted you at that time were blind and did not recognize that your major discovery was a wonderful theory that was unprecedented. (Naturally, you have always insisted on your discovery and have not been swayed by public opinion—such courage is even more admirable.) Why sigh? Because the Chinese academic world has had your "major discovery," it should be studied together, and your method of "investigating Mo Di's nationality" should be promoted and expanded. Or a few more nationalities of pre-Qin philosophers could be investigated, or a few great people in the political and academic worlds of the world could be investigated to be of Chinese nationality. Wouldn't this be a great event in the troubled world, admired by all nations? However, unfortunately, the Chinese people have forgotten it as if it were a light smoke. In just two or three years, your "discovery" has no longer been mentioned by anyone. Even though you have compiled a book called "A Study of Mo Di," the academic world turns a blind eye to it. If it weren't for me suddenly being inspired like a divine being to involve this so-called "Mo Di problem" (unfortunately, I still forgot your name), and you took the initiative to write a special letter to request correction and apology, then wouldn't your unique learning be buried in vain? Therefore, after apologizing, I am even more than willing to "correct" and promote it in the newspaper.

Furthermore, in the "Literary Weekly" in 1930, someone named "Mo Di" suddenly stole your, Mr. Hu's, "method of investigating Mo Di's return to nationality" and discovered that you, Mr. Hu, were also Indian! This confused me! I don't know if this discovery has the same value as your, Mr. Hu's, discovery? I dare not judge rashly, so I take the opportunity of apologizing and correcting to sincerely ask for guidance (it is indeed asking for guidance, not ridicule).

Finally, your letter said, "If you do not publish this letter of mine, then I can only spend money to publish an advertisement in Shenbao." I think you, sir, are slightly miscalculating. I have a suggestion: Since you, sir, are prepared to spend money to publish an advertisement, then when the country is in serious trouble and it is time to save the country through aviation, why not donate the advertisement fee to the Aviation Association? And you, sir, can also make a high-profile call to gather strength and come up with a "Mo Di Problem" plane, which would be conducive to saving the country and promoting unique learning. Would you, sir, be interested? I am willing to provide free publicity. I humbly apologize, correct, ask for guidance, offer advice, and wait for

Sincerely! Yours truly, Xuan, a contributor to Free Talk.

Our Troops Adopt Defensive Posture at Gubeikou 226

Our Troops Launch Flanking Attack on Enemy from Certain Pass

Japanese Side Increases Two Divisions to Assist in Battle

Mutō to Personally Command in Jinzhou

According to military dispatches from Beiping, our troops, due to the extended battle lines of enemy troops outside the pass, have decided to adopt a defensive posture at the front of Gubeikou. Other units, such as Unit X and Unit Y, have been dispatched to launch a flanking attack on the enemy from a certain pass. A major battle is expected in the next few days. Mutō, due to the defeat in the Great Wall battles, has decided to increase two divisions to assist the Japanese army in the attack. Mutō will also personally command in Jinzhou. (Special Dispatch, 16th)

The war clouds over Jinzhou and Xifengkou are growing more urgent. Chinese troops seize opportunities to attack and have successively invaded Rehe Province from the passes near Lengkou. Japanese air units mobilized yesterday to bomb, and the Nakamura unit, advancing towards Xifengkou, clashed with a Chinese army group lying in ambush 30 kilometers from Lengkou, resulting in a fierce four-hour battle. (Dispatch from Electric Communications Agency, 16th)

Since the counterattack by Song Zheyuan's troops against Xifengkou and Kuancheng on the 13th dealt a serious blow to the Japanese army, news of the Japanese army's defeat has spread throughout Japan. The general Japanese public initially doubted it, but then the Japanese military and the "Manchukuo" successively issued threatening statements, saying that if the Chinese army attacked Rehe again, Japan and Manchukuo would retaliate by invading Pingjin. Moreover, military advisory officials meetings have been held continuously in recent days. From this overall inspection, it can be confirmed that the Japanese army's repeated threats are actually evidence of the Japanese army suffering great losses in Xifengkou. (Dispatch from China United Press, 16th)

At noon on the 15th, Chinese troops in Jinzhou attacked the Matsuo Noeda unit and were temporarily repulsed, but then counterattacked, eventually establishing an attack base for the Chinese troops. The distance between the Chinese and Japanese armies is now only 1,000 meters, and the situation is inevitably deteriorating. (Dispatch from Japan United Press, 11th)

According to telegrams from foreigners in Xinjiang via Beiping, the disturbances in Xinjiang have developed seriously. Aksu's Old City has been captured by rebels. The Chinese army was defeated, and reinforcements have been dispatched to the troubled area. (Dispatch from Reuters, 16th)

League of Nations Advisory Committee Holds Meeting Yesterday, US Representative Receives Warm Welcome 228

It is Presumed that the Norwegian Representative will Serve as Chairman

Two Subcommittees Have Been Formed

To Study Arms Embargo and the Puppet State Issue

The twenty-one member advisory committee organized by the League of Nations General Assembly to handle the Sino-Japanese dispute convened at 3:30 PM today, lasting for two hours and fifteen minutes. After the assembly accepted the US government's reply, an attendant was sent to invite Mr. Wilson, the US representative waiting upstairs, to the venue. After a few minutes of waiting, Wilson arrived at the venue, and the assembly cheered. Following this, the issue of the chairman was discussed. The former chairman of the Nineteenth Committee, Belgian representative Hymans, is no longer in Geneva, and his position is being temporarily filled by Belgian representative Paul-Boncour. Paul-Boncour repeatedly stated that Belgium did not wish to continue holding the chairmanship and suggested that the position should be held by a representative of a major power. Swiss representative Motta suggested that the major powers should take turns serving as chairman, but both Britain and France were not prepared to accept the above two suggestions. As a result, Norwegian representative Lange was elected chairman. At this point, the assembly discussed possible ways for the US representative to cooperate, as the US representative does not participate in voting according to the US government's decision. Next, the assembly discussed the issue of arms shipments to the Far East. On the suggestion of British representative Eden, a subcommittee was appointed on the spot to study the matter. The powers of this subcommittee are very broad and unlimited. Although the issue of an arms embargo has been discussed, it has not been implemented. Irish representative Lester suggested that appropriate actions should be studied based on the third paragraph of the draft resolution proposed by the Nineteenth Committee regarding the problems arising from the major powers' non-recognition of "Manchukuo." The League of Nations has apparently received a petition from "Manchukuo" to join the Postal and Telegraph and International Wireless Telegraph Alliances.

Furthermore, the issues of passports, stamps, and the status of consuls stationed in Manchuria will also follow. In order to inspect this and related issues, the twenty-one member committee decided to appoint a second subcommittee. The second subcommittee will study this matter and then propose solutions to the twenty-one member committee. The first subcommittee consists of eleven countries: Britain, France, Germany, Italy, the United States, Spain, Czechoslovakia, Sweden, Norway, Switzerland, and the Netherlands. The second subcommittee consists of twelve countries: Britain, France, Germany, Italy, the United States, Ireland, Turkey, the Netherlands, Spain, Sweden, Mexico, and Norway. (Reuters, 15th)

Japanese Espionage in Inner Mongolia's Xilin Gol League 261

Japan Has Already Planned to Invade the Xilin Gol League

Mongolian People Hope the Central Government Will Pay Attention to Mongolian Defense

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: The area of the three provinces of Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan, including Inner Mongolia, comprises the Jerim League in Rehe, the Xilin Gol League in Chahar, and the Yeke Zhaomeng League and Ulanqab League in Suiyuan in Inner Mongolia. These four leagues account for two-thirds of the area of the three provinces of Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan. Among the four leagues, the Xilin Gol League has the largest area, covering an estimated 15,000 li (approximately 7,500 kilometers). It has a population of 50,000. Japan's Manchurian-Mongolian policy not only seeks to annex the three northeastern provinces but also includes the three provinces of Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan. It is said that Japan has already planned to merge the various leagues of Inner Mongolia into a concrete puppet Manchurian state and then expand its military aggression to seize Outer Mongolia, a vast territory. Therefore, since the fall of Chengde, the Japanese army has advanced further, focusing on Chahar Province. Regarding the defense of Chahar Province, we have already made strict arrangements, and the security of Chahar Province is definitely not a concern. Deshixian, the League Leader of Xilin Gol League and concurrently Zasak Dorji of the Right Banner of Sonid, previously went to Nanjing to report on the recent situation of Xilin Gol League and border defense matters, providing detailed reports to the Central Government and the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, and met with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to explain everything. The Central Government and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek paid great attention to the defense of Inner Mongolia. Prince Deshixian stayed in Nanjing and Hankou for more than two months. After returning to Chahar a month ago, he went to various banners under the league to inspect them, representing the central government in appeasing the Mongolian people. The prince has now returned to Zhangyuan, but with the fall of Chengde, the Japanese army is actively plotting to invade western Inner Mongolia. To plan the defense of Inner Mongolia, the prince will go to Wutai in Shanxi within days to discuss everything with Zhangjia Hutuktu, the Pacification Commissioner of Inner Mongolia in Wutai, to avoid being caught unprepared. Recently, according to Deshixian's talk about the recent situation in Inner Mongolia, he briefly stated: "The eastern part of Inner Mongolia, from Hulunbuir to the Jerim League, has been completely lost. Now, the remaining western part of Inner Mongolia is under active threat from the Japanese. The current situation of the Xilin Gol League is precarious. After investigation, all the leagues of Inner Mongolia have long sincerely supported the Central Government. The Central Government should treat all leagues of Inner Mongolia equally and do its best to appease them so that they can be enlightened and know to serve the country. Some time ago, I went south and stayed in Nanjing for more than two months. I reported the situation of our league and Inner Mongolia to the Central Government in detail. The Central Government has appointed Zhangjia Hutuktu as the Pacification Commissioner of Inner Mongolia so that the people of Inner Mongolia can have a governing organ and avoid the Central Government feeling powerless. Recently, the national situation has become urgent. The people of Inner Mongolia all know to defend the territory and protect the country. However, due to the lack of equipment, even brave people and good horses are useless without sharp weapons. The area of the Xilin Gol League is 15,000 li, and the population is more than 50,000. The Central Government has issued only more than 100 firearms. It is more than enough to protect the local area, but it is really insufficient to defend against foreign aggression. If the Japanese army invades, there is a tendency to drive straight in. Western Inner Mongolia is helpless and can only be invaded by the Japanese army. Therefore, the anti-Japanese plan should pay attention to the defense of Inner Mongolia. The Mongolian people are good at riding and shooting, and Inner Mongolia produces good horses. The Central Government should organize Mongolian cavalry, issue firearms, and provide short-term training, which can achieve great effectiveness. Using them to defend the Mongolian border and assist in the anti-Japanese war will definitely be effective. The Mongolian people will definitely not be used by the Japanese." (March 8)

Various Worries About China After Japan's Withdrawal from the League of Nations 262

Worry that the Hot War Will Expand to North China

Worry that China Will Not Let Japan Expand

Worry that Commerce Will Fall into an Impasse

Worry about League of Nations Sanctions

Worry about the United States and Russia Uniting Against Japan

Tokyo's Kokumin Shimbun published an article by Nagano Ro on the 9th, entitled "A Study of Japan's Relations with China After Withdrawing from the League of Nations." The points mentioned in the article are very pertinent. A translated version is provided below for those who are concerned about national affairs.

How will the relationship between China and Japan be after Japan withdraws from the League of Nations? It depends on the actions of the League itself and the development of the war in Rehe. If the war in Rehe does not affect North China, then the League will not have a major adverse impact. However, given the current situation in China, it is difficult to predict whether the war will affect North China. What policies the League will adopt toward Japan also depends on the expansion of the war, which will have a major impact on Japan's relationship with China in the future.

The scope of relations with China is quite broad. In addition to China and Japan, there are other powers involved. First, let's observe the relations between China and Japan. Since the Wanbaoshan Incident the year before last, China has been constantly rejecting Japanese goods. Although the Lytton Report mentions the rejection of Japan, the League of Nations also tends to legitimize China's rejection of Japan. If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, then the momentum of legitimizing the rejection of Japan will inevitably become stronger. Today, China's rejection of Japan has become an open secret. If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, will the League adopt sanctions? If economic blockade cannot be implemented, then what measures will be taken? Japan's major issue at present is the weapons issue. The raw materials for Japanese manufacturing have always been supplied by China. Recently, the supply of the Yawata Iron Mine from Daye has been cut off and replaced by imports from Southeast Asia, so there is no need to worry. However, China imposes high tariffs on Japanese goods to prevent the import of Japanese goods. At the same time, taking advantage of the deterioration of Japanese-American trade, China's raw silk exports to the United States are very prosperous and attempts to contract silk industry and improve quality. This is one of the impacts suffered by the Japanese silk industry. Next, if the war spreads to North China after Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, the League will regard it as an act of war. At this time, the relationship between China and Japan will have to change. Among them, whether the Sino-Japanese Treaty of Commerce and Navigation will be declared abolished or revised by China due to the expiration of the old treaty is also a major issue. Whether the unilateral declaration of abolition can take effect is also a question. If Japanese in China are treated as people from non-treaty countries, then the issue of extraterritoriality will inevitably conflict with the issue of concessions. The Japanese residing in the mainland and the enterprises run by Japanese will inevitably be severely hit. At that time, Japanese will inevitably concentrate in the main coastal commercial ports. Therefore, it is speculated that Japan's trade with China and various enterprises will only concentrate in commercial ports such as Tianjin, Qingdao, Shanghai, and Hankou. However, whether the Hankou area can be maintained is still a question. In short, the deterioration of relations with China depends greatly on the future situation and whether the military situation in Rehe spreads to North China. Today, the relations between China and Japan are very bad. The economic relations between China and Japan will fall into a more difficult situation, which goes without saying. Therefore, we must have full preparation for the domestic industrial policy in order to advance into China in the future. This is the second thing that the people of the country have to worry about.

As for the movements of the League of Nations, it is because it coincides with the era of the change of the President of the United States, and the US foreign policy has not yet been clarified. In addition, the war situation in Rehe has not yet spread to North China, and Japan and the League of Nations have not substantially severed relations. If the war situation in Rehe stops here, then both the active and passive factions of the League of Nations will not take major actions. Because when the Chinese resistance spreads to the Tianjin area, the powers will regard it as a formal war, which may cause major entanglements. If the League of Nations hesitates and watches, China will also declare the severance of diplomatic relations. At this time, whether the League of Nations has concrete plans is unknown. At present, direct negotiations between China and Japan seem impossible, then the relationship between China and Japan will become a semi-permanent struggle. Wouldn't Japan's trade with China be in a more tragic situation? At the same time, the powers take advantage of the unfavorable situation of Japan's business and trade, and mutually advance into the Far East, and Japan's trade position is even more unimaginable.

From the perspective of international relations, the United States and China have long been jointly dealing with Japan since the Russo-Japanese War. Although the United States does not dare to confront Japan by force today, the United States' provision of funds and weapons to China is tantamount to killing Japanese by Chinese hands. At the same time, the communist army of Russia, taking advantage of the conflict between China and Japan, advanced into Manchuria to contain Japan. What is most noteworthy is that the assumption of office of US President Roosevelt is not far from recognizing Soviet Russia. In the future, the United States and Russia will be in the same vein, then the situation in the Far East will inevitably undergo new changes. From the above observations, it is of interest and worth studying how the powers in this complex relationship will change the Chinese stage in the future.

Disputes over the Contract for Tea Tax Collection in Southern Anhui 263

The Director-General Was Beaten and Seriously Injured

Wuhu Correspondence: After the Finance Department divided the business tax of tea in the whole province into two regions, Southern Anhui and Northern Anhui, it recruited merchants to handle it. There were eight bureaus in Southern Anhui. The Wuhu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Joint Association telegraphed the Finance Department to allow the association to handle it. However, the Finance Department recently adopted a bidding method. As a result, it was decided to appoint Cao Qibang as the Director-General of the eight tea tax bureaus in Southern Anhui. The subordinate branch bureaus were re-contracted by various merchants. Zhang Yizhai in Yi County, Ye Zhuomin in Xiuyu, Yu Qiheng in Qimen, Yu Guangxi in Wuyuan, Hong Meiyao in Tongshi, Cui Lianggong in Jingtai, and Cao Qibang, the Director-General, concurrently handled Xuanlang Guang. After investigation, the total amount of tea tax in Southern Anhui is 52,800 yuan. The first installment of 35,000 yuan in cash should be prepaid, but it has not been fully paid yet. The Finance Department is strictly urging the full payment of the ratio. However, the merchants who contracted the tax had a dispute with the Director-General due to too few branch bureaus and uneven distribution. Unexpectedly, a conflict occurred yesterday, resulting in a fight. Cao Qibang was seriously injured. It is unknown how it will be resolved. (13th)

The Northwest Line of Eurasia Decides to Expand to Xinjiang Within This Month 267

Li Jingcong Will Determine the Schedule for His Trip to Xinjiang After Returning South

The Guangdong-Hankou Line Will Be Trial-Sailed Next Month and Will Be Extended to Luoyang

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, regarding the westward expansion of the main line of Eurasia Aviation Corporation and the preparations for the new Guangdong-Hankou line, Mr. Cha Zhenhu, an employee of the company, told reporters this morning:

Trial Flight of Guangdong-Hankou: Eurasia and China Aviation Corporation have both opened up the Guangdong-Hankou line. China Aviation flies from Shanghai to Guangzhou, and Eurasia flies from Hankou to Guangzhou. Eurasia's main business is to transport international mail. Strictly speaking, it cannot transport domestic mail. However, because there are no other company's planes flying on the existing routes, it also transports domestic mail. The opening of the Guangdong-Hankou line is also for the purpose of absorbing international mail. It is planned to start the trial flight at the beginning of next month. The original plan was to extend it from Hankou to Luoyang to connect with the main line of Eurasia.

Borrowing Airports: Due to the company's limited resources, the Guangdong-Hankou airport facilities in Xiangyang, Hankou, Changsha, and Guangzhou are not purchased by the company itself. The company borrows the original government airports and builds a few houses. The same is true for Nanjing and Luoyang on the main line. Xi'an, Lanzhou, Suzhou, etc., are all opened by the local government.

Connecting to Dihua: After the Eurasia main line once opened to Dihua last year, the Xinjiang Provincial Government later built a radio station, and the flight was too risky, so it could not be expanded to the west. Now the Executive Yuan has ordered the Xinjiang Provincial Government to comply. However, transportation is inconvenient, and telegrams take ten days to return. The company previously received a telegram from Xinjiang Province stating that the local area was unstable and the westward flight was temporarily postponed. However, the company decided to fly to Dihua this month to install a radio to complete the Eurasia route. Manager Li Jingcong's trip to Beiping is also related to this. Li will return to Shanghai on the 19th and can decide on the date of his trip to Xinjiang.
