Meeting Minutes of the Northern and Southern Rice Groups 274

The Shanghai Bean and Rice Trade Association held the first plenary meeting of the Northern and Southern Rice Groups at the Cuixiu Hall in Yuyuan Garden in the city at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. More than 100 members from the north and south attended. Chairman Zhu Zixiang presided over the meeting. After the meeting began, Chairman Zhu reported that since the establishment of the group, this is the first meeting of this session. After discussing and regulating the industry rules, all members have been able to abide by the regulations, and business performance has been good. However, a few stores are still thinking about undermining the regulations of the association, so it is appropriate to discuss practical measures to deal with them. The letter from the rural co-workers in the south of the city stated that the rural business is slightly different from that of this street, etc. It was decided that the rural group leaders Yang Yinggang and Zhang Yinnan should handle it. The members discussed each item (1) The date and time of the group's plenary meeting, it was decided to hold meetings at 3:00 PM on the 2nd and 16th of each month (1) After that, it was stipulated that the chairman should be the general affairs group leader of the north and south (1) It was stipulated that the commission for foreign rice should be increased. It was decided that the commission should be increased by 15 cents for every 200 pounds. Each mark should be at least 50 bags. If there are a small number of bags, add 20 cents. The balance should be settled at the end of the month, and all discounts should be included. If there are violations, deal with them in the same way as the Hedong rice (1) Report on the dispute over the bucket rice. It was decided that the bucket master should declare in the Social Bureau that he should weigh the rice accurately, so as not to be used as an excuse by others (1) Review the commission issue, it was decided that the commission for cash transactions should be 6 points, limited to 5 days. Those who exceed the deadline should be 3 points. All balances must be settled at the end of the month. The meeting adjourned, and it was six o'clock.

The Annual Reports of the Various Departments of the Municipal Council 275

The Park Management Department: Last year, the Hongkou Park was expanded by 21 acres and prepared as a sports field. A tree nursery was added at the corner of Jiangwan Road and Huishan Road. Many modifications were made to the Waiqiao Park, and a summer shelter was specially built. Trees were planted and children's sports equipment was added to the children's playground on Nanyang Road. The Hongkou Park was closed and reopened on March 19. There were 120,000 sports fields for football, baseball, softball, lawn tennis, etc., 88 tennis courts, 9 racecourses, and one golf course. A sports field was also set up in Huishan Park, where the lawn tennis court is the best. A total of 85 concerts were held in the parks. Zhaofeng Park was the most popular, and the zoo was often crowded, with a total of 780,000 visitors throughout the year. Statistics for each park show that there were a total of approximately 2.1 million visitors throughout the year. This number is slightly less than in 1931, because Hongkou Park was closed, which greatly reduced the number of visitors.

The Chinese Language Department: The foreign staff of the Municipal Council learn Chinese, either the Beijing language or the local language. Therefore, there is a Chinese language department. During the martial law period last year, classes were suspended. Afterwards, the Deputy Director of the Department led 22 Chinese teachers and joined the Chinese team of the business community and were assigned to various defense troops to serve as interpreters. Therefore, the defense troops and the residents were not isolated. The teaching method of the department is the direct method. Usually, students can complete their studies in three years, and some can graduate in less than three years. In addition, the Chinese documents received by the Municipal Council are translated into English by the department. The full text of the gazette and annual reports are translated from English to Chinese by the department. The Public Library: At the end of the year, the Public Library of the Municipal Council had 308 annual members, 175 half-year members, 103 three-month members, and 4 one-month members, for a total of 590 people. In total, 58,347 books were borrowed throughout the year, and 16,576 people read in the reading room. Since August, a fine of one cent per day has been imposed for overdue books, which has greatly increased the circulation of books. A total of 498 new books were purchased this year, including 298 novels, 109 non-fiction books, and 91 children's books. Every Saturday from 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM, a special time is set for children's story reading.

The Information Department: The Information Department of the Municipal Council was established in the winter of 1931. In 1932, more than 30 newspapers, news agencies, and correspondents in this city and other cities regularly received documents published by the Department. The newspapers included Chinese newspapers, English newspapers, Japanese newspapers, and French, German, and Russian newspapers. A total of 420 published documents were issued throughout the year, including summaries of events to be handled by the Municipal Council, resolutions of the Municipal Council and the reasons for them, and the work situation and reports of various departments of the Municipal Council. If special information is needed regarding the work of the Municipal Council, the Department will provide it at any time.

The Three Principles of the KMT Party Headquarters in Shanghai and Seven Counties Rectify the Charitable Properties of the Seven Counties 276

Shanghai County Sends Personnel to Express Their Views

Five Improvement Plans Will Be Discussed at the Meeting

The KMT Party Headquarters in Shanghai, Songjiang, Nanhui, Chuansha, Jinshan, Fengxian, Qingpu, and other seven counties of the old Song prefecture, in view of the fact that the administrative power of the seven-county charitable properties belongs to the people of the seven counties and is now monopolized by a few people, which is illegal, and that the charitable undertakings held over the years only have the Puji, Yuying, and Quanjie halls, which are simple in equipment and corrupt in content, the seven-county party headquarters proposed rectification at this provincial congress, which was approved and the provincial party headquarters sent a letter to the provincial government. The Shanghai County Party Headquarters recently sent Executive Committee members Peng Liren and Jin Zuobao, and Supervisory Committee member Zhang Yi to Songjiang to inspect the Puji and Yuying halls together with representatives of the Songjiang County Party Headquarters. They have now returned to Shanghai. Inspector Peng Liren published the inspection process and improvement opinions yesterday, and distributed them to the seven county party headquarters for a regular meeting to discuss them. The following is a record:

Inspection Results 277

This time, I, along with comrades Jin and Zhang, went to Songjiang to first inspect the Pujitang, Yuyingtang, and Quanjietang. The Pujitang is a home specifically for the elderly. The elderly inside are dressed in ragged, filthy clothes. They eat only a bowl of cold rice each meal, and receive one copper coin per day, barely enough to buy a piece of tofu. They sleep on straw and old cotton batting without any beds. The air is foul. The elderly cry out for help, their misery unbearable to witness, making it impossible to stay long. The lives of the elderly being cared for are truly worse than those of prisoners or beggars. We then went to the Yuyingtang for a detailed inspection, but were also unsatisfied. Regulations stipulate that one wet nurse should feed two infants, but the home often has one nurse feeding three. The nurses frequently fall ill, and all facilities fail to meet sanitary standards, resulting in most of the infants being unable to thrive. We did not have time to visit the Quanjietang, but it fundamentally does not align with modern trends and should be thoroughly reformed. Based on the findings of the inspection, I propose the following improvement plan:

Adding Board Members 278

(1) The current charitable board of directors has thirty members who exist in name only and are generally not responsible. Only a few individuals control it, leading to rampant corruption. It is proposed to add six more members, one from each county except Songjiang, for a total of thirty-six. They will be divided into twelve groups by lottery, with three members per group, serving as monthly directors. Each group must reside in the association to oversee general affairs and inspect the conditions of each hall at any time. After this, only one general meeting will be held each year to decide the year's plan of action and budget, review the past year's accounts, and publish a report to be widely distributed to all sectors of the seven counties to ensure fairness.

Popular Election of Directors 279

(2) Currently, the directors are all decided by the county governments, which send letters to the Songjiang County government requesting appointments. The county government only approaches the gentry. Although there may be honest and impartial commoners suitable for charitable directors, the county government has no way of knowing. It is proposed that, before the popular election of county heads, these directors be elected by the county representatives' assembly. There should be no restrictions on party membership. After the election, the county party headquarters will send a letter to the county government requesting the issuance of certificates. In the future, when county heads are popularly elected, these directors will be elected at the same time as the county head. Only in this way can public opinion be widely solicited and charitable funds properly managed.

Defining the Boundaries of the Three Halls 280

(3) Currently, the boundaries of the three halls are clearly defined, leading to a relative shortage of funds for the Pujitang, causing the elderly to suffer mistreatment. The lack of funds is also one of the reasons. Previously, each county distributed these charitable funds. Songjiang County argues that it is an integral whole and cannot be divided. However, the three halls all serve the cause of charity. Why can't there be overall planning? In the future, the boundaries of the three halls should be broken down, and separate plans and budgets should be set. The Pujitang should be renamed as a nursing home. While it may not be able to provide fine silk clothing and rich meat, it must ensure that the elderly are well-fed and warmly clothed.

Establishing a Daycare Center 281

(4) The Yuyingtang should establish a daycare center. In addition to continuing to care for orphaned and impoverished infants, infants of female workers or impoverished families whose mothers cannot breastfeed or care for them due to the need to earn a living should be allowed to be placed in the center. This will promote new endeavors to meet the needs of modern society.

Re-establishing a Women's Vocational School 282

(5) The Quanjietang should be transformed into a women's vocational training school. All virtuous women from wealthy families currently housed there should be ordered to return home. Those without property and unable to support themselves should be transferred to the training school. Other unemployed women should be recruited into the school and taught various skills suitable for women, as well as common knowledge and basic literacy, so that women can be self-reliant and promote the realization of equal economic status between men and women.

One Mouth Cannot Overcome Three 283

Lovers Arrested and Sent to Court

Li Xiuying, a nineteen-year-old woman from Taixing, residing at a certain address on Jishi Fei Road in the Chinese Settlement, possesses some beauty. She used to work as a female laborer in the Gongda Cotton Mill in Yangshupu. Recently, she fell in love with Ma Yueting, a twenty-four-year-old man from Shandong. Their hearts were in tune, filled with affection. On the eighteenth of last month, Ma lured her to No. 272 Huasheng Road (inside the Gongda Cotton Mill's factory housing) and they began living together as husband and wife. The other day, her elder brother, Li Baixiang, discovered their hiding place and reported the situation to the Municipal Police Bureau, which dispatched detective Zhao Caoqiao to the Yulin Road Police Station, requesting assistance in the arrest. The patrol chief sent detective Gui Shou to secretly investigate the address, arrest Ma, and bring Li Xiuying with him to the police station. The patrol chief ordered Ma Yueting to be detained, and Li was handed over to her brother Li Baixiang to take home. This morning, Ma was sent to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, recounted the events, stating that Li Xiuying claimed to be twenty-two years old at the police station, but her brother insisted she was nineteen. Li stated that she willingly lived with the defendant. The police station had no objection to the Public Security Bureau's request to extradite the defendant, but requested that an official letter be submitted afterward. Li Baixiang then testified that his sister, Xiuying, was indeed nineteen years old and had been betrothed to someone last winter in their hometown. Li Xiuying insisted that she was twenty-two years old, born in the Year of the Rat, and that her parents had passed away. She claimed that she willingly fell in love with the defendant and did not know that her brothers had betrothed her to someone else. The court asked, "Your three brothers testified that you are nineteen years old." The woman replied, "They are three mouths, and I only have one. I cannot argue. I must let them say what they want." The defendant testified that Li Xiuying willingly followed him to be his wife and that he did not abduct her. They had only been in a relationship for about a month. Furthermore, her brothers and sisters had visited his home before, asking for his judgment. Detective Zhao Caoqiao testified that the family did not report her missing to the bureau at the time and did not know the inside story. He requested that the extradition report be submitted. Judge Wu Zehan ordered Ma Yueting to be handed over to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

The Case of the Notorious Bandit Is Heard 284

Zhou Yong'an, also known as Zhai Yong'an, a notorious bandit from Qingjiang, opened fire on Liyuan Road in the two cities on July 28 of last year, killing Municipal Public Security Bureau police officer Zhang Hanchen and wounding police officer Sun Jiming. He also robbed Sun's pistol. Public Security Bureau detectives arrested Zhou and sent him to Nanjing, searching for the robbed pistol. However, Zhou took the opportunity to escape, removed his handcuffs, and fled to Shanghai. Despite a strict search, he was not apprehended. On the thirteenth of this month, at noon, Chinese Detective Chief Liu Junqing of the Old Patrol Station received a tip and arrested Zhou in the Shenjiatan area of Yangshupu. A pistol and four bullets were found at No. 80 Bailu Road in Zhabei. He was sent to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. This morning, Criminal Court President Feng Shide opened a court session for further questioning. The patrol station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that the Municipal Public Security Bureau had sent personnel to the case today and requested extradition, to which the patrol station did not object. The representative of the Municipal Public Security Bureau submitted an official letter requesting permission to extradite Zhou. After questioning Zhou briefly, Judge Feng ordered him to be handed over to the Public Security Bureau personnel to be taken back for further investigation. The case of the notorious bandit is being heard.

Liu A'gen et al. Chinese Detective Chen Yonggui and 包探 Wang Jiaju of the Old Patrol Station previously arrested the bandits Liu A'gen, Lu Peiqing, Weng A'xiao, Gu A'si, Feng Yuanchang, Li Jinbiao, Yu Songshan, Xu Xuesheng, and Feng Si, confiscating two pistols, seven bullets, one gold ring, twenty-one pawn tickets, and one fur robe. They were sent to the Special Court for interrogation and detention. This morning, the court continued the interrogation. The patrol station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that the defendants were found to have no crimes in Shanghai but had committed multiple armed robberies in Kunshan. Today, the Public Security Bureau of Kunshan County sent personnel to request extradition, to which the patrol station had no objection. The court should review the case according to the law. The leader of the investigation team of the Public Security Bureau of Kunshan County, Jiang Fachang, submitted the case and presented an official letter requesting permission to extradite the defendants. Judge Feng Shide questioned the defendants one by one and ordered them to be handed over to the Kunshan County personnel to be taken back for investigation, along with the stolen goods.

Page 23

Comments

Why This Treatment of Koreans? 285

— Tianfang

Recently, a bizarre kidnapping case occurred in Shanghai. The kidnapped victim was Li Chunshan, a Korean independence party leader who had become a naturalized Chinese citizen. The kidnappers were "short bandits" who used a "black-plated car." Although the truth has not yet been fully revealed, if we are not forgetful, we can recall the political kidnapping cases in the French Concession after the "January 28th Incident" as a comparison. The significance is far greater than the assault of a few foreign monks, nor is it limited to the kidnapping of a millionaire. It directly concerns our national system.

According to Li, he moved from the French Concession to the Nanshi area for "security reasons." Unfortunately, this "precaution" was a mistake. One should seek security within the walls of the strong. All we have to offer is "apologies." Although we are very conscientious towards the nationals of belligerent countries—probably out of the lingering sentiment of "not capturing the two old men"—as for naturalized citizens, well, we can't even manage our own people. Those who are bullied abroad are bullied by their own people at home. What does it matter if these "brothers" of the same ancestry but different nationality suffer?

Based on Li's accomplishments in Korea, he may have hopes of being called a "national father" in the future, but he is not as fortunate as our "national father." Sun Yat-sen also suffered in London! A memorial is still in place, but he eventually gained freedom. What about Li? He has been kidnapped for four or five days, and his whereabouts are still unknown. He may have been sent to a prison thousands of miles away. The actions are similar, but the results are different. The only difference is that Shanghai is not London, and the ghostly tricks of the X country are far superior to those of the Manchu government.

Now that the incident has occurred, it cannot be denied that the authorities' protection was insufficient, such as the scarcity of police posts. However, this trend cannot be allowed to continue. For the safety of naturalized citizens and to restore national prestige, the authorities must bring the culprits to justice in the shortest possible time, or at least tell us the reason why they cannot be brought to justice.

Literature and Art

Miscellaneous Poems on Current Affairs 286

— Deng Niukun

Red calamities everywhere have not yet recovered, heavy rains in Jiangcheng urge for taxes, the people's livelihood is used to being like catkins in the wind, turning into snow and drifting like duckweed.

I once heard of the dwarfed invaders looting the rivers and mountains, the men of the Northeast surrounding themselves with knives, even if their neck blood cannot return an inch of land, they have left righteousness in the world.

Last night, the wind and rain often startled the vines, Chengde inexplicably reported the loss of the city, where have the tens of thousands of brave soldiers gone, Zhang Qing of Tianjin and Ping lay high and unconcerned.

Why execute Yu Lin for the lost land, the golden Northeast is abandoned like a mat, the broken walls of Jiangnan are still there today, it is possible to move troops to be neighbors.

The national decree has not been enforced for many years, there has never been law before the military, now that we feel the danger of doom, both jade and stone will be burned together, how can the tiles be spared.

The Money Overflowing from Beautiful Clothing 287

— Qun

Someone's Sister 288

— Binfu

It was a beautiful afternoon. My older brother and I were planning to take my nephew, Rongshu, to the Great World. Because my older brother was moving, my sisters-in-law were busy packing, filling the room with dark, useless things. We felt extremely annoyed, and Rongshu's shouting interfered with their work, so we decided to go to the Great World. As soon as the decision was made, Rongshu was overjoyed. Suddenly, the neighbor downstairs announced that a female guest wanted to see me. I responded and ran downstairs. At the top of the stairs, I saw a woman from the dark light, already reaching out and across two steps of the stairs. To identify the guest and to prevent my guest from falling in the dark, I turned around and immediately turned on the light. Unexpectedly, the face of the middle-aged woman that came from the electric light still did not seem familiar to me, but the unfamiliar and smiling face had already safely come to my front, and greeted me cordially, "Mr. Feng doesn't recognize me, does he?"

I desperately concentrated my brainpower and carefully looked at her whole body. Her hair was thick, her face was oval, her cheekbones were high, her cheongsam was made of green Indian satin, and her accent was from Shaoxing. Who is this?

"Yes, I can't remember! Haha"

"I'm SW's sister. Have you forgotten the night you came to my house?"

"Ah, yes, yes. My memory is really bad." Only then did I realize that we had been standing there for a long time, so I quickly found a chair in the mess of boxes and asked her to sit down apologetically.

looked over, but she was caught by her sharp eyes, and called to sit on his lap, so the conversation shifted to her and Rongshu. As a result, Rongshu thought that the watch on her wrist was very beautiful and asked to take it off to play. I immediately forbade him, and he climbed down and returned to the inside room in disappointment.

"This child is really smart and lively. It's a pity that I'm in a hurry and didn't buy any food."

The conversation shifted back to SW, because SW was ultimately the link between me and this female guest.

"SW really knows how to spend money. The money he brought when school started has already been used up. He is not as frugal as you, Mr. Feng."

SW is my very good classmate. He is from Shaoxing. One night half a year ago, we were late for the train in Yuyao, and I went to his older sister's house with his sister-in-law, the bureau chief. His older sister treated us very kindly. However, the older sister I saw under the kerosene lamp at that time was somewhat vague in my memory. My heart was filled with the shame of not being a good host, and I really didn't know what to say.

It was the capable her who spoke first; "I went to see my younger brother today, and his stomach problems have flared up again. He is lying in bed, so he couldn't come to see you with me." The reply was just a low "Yes, yes, yes." I really couldn't think of anything to say.

"I came from Suzhou last night, and I went to the school in Wusong early in the morning to see my younger brother, but unexpectedly he fell ill again. This person's health is really not good, and being a guest in a foreign land makes people very worried. Mr. Feng, your health seems to be very good."

As I paced in circles, I peeked through the side door at my older brother and the others who were waiting. At this time, Rongshu had come to ask several times. My older brother knew that this female guest intended to "talk for a long time," so he took off his hat that he had put on.

The conversation was silent for a while, and Rongshu came to make trouble again. I was a little confused by this unexpected praise.

"I came to Shanghai from Yuyao the day before yesterday, and I went to Suzhou yesterday, because he is now doing a job in Suzhou. Unexpectedly, he had just been transferred to Hangzhou when I arrived in Suzhou. I had to stay in a hotel in Suzhou overnight, planning to transfer to Hangzhou from Shanghai this morning, but..." Her words suddenly stopped, and just as I was about to ask, her words burst out again.

"Anyway, you are my younger brother's old friend, so it doesn't hurt to say it. You know that my travel bag was not very full to begin with. After this unexpected delay, I completely ran out of money. I was going to go to my younger brother to get the money when I arrived in Shanghai, but unexpectedly he didn't have a penny either. Aren't you angry?"

"Yes, he probably bought books. Foreign books are really expensive now." I explained for my friend.

"That's right, so he told me your address and asked me to borrow from you temporarily. After I arrive in Hangzhou, I will send it back to you immediately, and I also want to send some to my younger brother."

"Very good, very good. How much?"
